Special Publication

The Red Peril and China's Survival

— (Yang Xingfo)

Since the Xinhai Revolution, although the Qing Dynasty was quickly overthrown, the ideals of the revolution have yet to be realized. In the past twenty years, there have been countless internal wars between warlords, and between warlords and revolutionary forces. Now, before the task of unification is completed, the unprecedented Red Peril in Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan has become a prairie fire. People are accustomed to hearing about internal wars. Those who reside in bandit areas and suffer firsthand pain cry out in agony, while those who are fortunate enough to live in Jiangsu and Zhejiang or reside in concessions mostly view it with indifference, as if they were Yue people viewing Qin people. They do not realize that today's Red Army, backed by the Third International and Soviet Russia, has a strict party-government-military organization. Killing and arson are planned, and rape and plunder have become doctrines. They are by no means comparable to the bandits of past dynasties or the warlords of recent times. Can a moribund and collapsing patriarchal society possibly escape this cruel and rigorous Red influence? Therefore, although today's Red Peril is concentrated in Jiangxi and spreading to neighboring provinces such as Hubei and Hunan, the hidden danger is actually pervasive throughout the country. At a time when foreign aggression is rampant, there is also the danger of Red infiltration at the core. The survival of the nation hangs by a thread. I hope that my compatriots who live in peace and prosperity will spare some time from their leisurely pursuits to deeply contemplate this situation.

In the past, the people's ignorance of the Red Peril cannot be solely blamed on their slowness to react. The government and the military also cannot shirk their responsibility for inaccurate reports that concealed the truth and glossed over the situation. This kind of dishonest propaganda not only gave the people a false impression but also often became the main reason for the military's failure to suppress the Red bandits. When Liu Jianxu, the commander of the Hunan division, was in charge of pacifying the Red bandits in Pingxiang and Liuyang, he issued nine points of instruction to all anti-bandit troops in the province, the first of which was: [False military intelligence is a bad habit of the military. Recent investigations have found that all the reports of victory in engagements between the army and the bandits are often fabricated and exaggerated. They either claim to have seized a certain number of guns or to have annihilated countless bandits. However, when verified against the facts, they are often inconsistent. The military must rely on intelligence to plan its operations. False intelligence will inevitably lead to misjudgment and hinder military progress. This should be emphasized and heeded.] The news reported on June 20 of this year [Commander-in-Chief Chiang ordered that the military dispatches from various anti-bandit units mostly report victories and no defeats, and that the higher-level officials are separated from the actual situation of the bandits due to false reports of military intelligence, which makes it difficult to make decisive plans. On the 28th, he strictly ordered all troops to earnestly correct this.] All of these are sufficient proof of the failure of anti-bandit propaganda in the past. The spread of the Red Peril is more than enough to bring about the downfall of China. Although the superficial suppression depends on the military's force, the fundamental clarification will not succeed without enlightened politics and a sound society. Moreover, it is even more essential to awaken the masses to face the great crisis together and achieve the effect of nationwide fortification and resurrection.

A brief history: The rampant rise of bandits and rebels is a natural product of political changes and social chaos in past dynasties. In the Han Dynasty, there were the Green Forest and Red Eyebrow rebellions and the Yellow Turban Rebellion. In the Tang Dynasty, there were the rebellions of Wang Xianzhi and Huang Chao. In the Song Dynasty, there were the exploits of Song Jiang and his thirty-six followers. In the Yuan Dynasty, there were the Red Turban rebels. In the Ming Dynasty, there were the roving bandits of Li Zicheng and Zhang Xianzhong. In the Qing Dynasty, there were the White Lotus rebels in Sichuan and Hubei and the Nian rebels. The smaller ones caused temporary disasters and devastated the people, while the larger ones led to the downfall of dynasties and the change of dynasties, becoming the main cause of the rise and fall of generations. However, at that time, Chinese culture was superior to neighboring ethnic groups. The outbreak of banditry was mostly due to overpopulation, agricultural disasters, or government mismanagement. No matter how the social order was destroyed, there was no conflict or change of thought and system. Therefore, the so-called downfall of a dynasty was actually the rise and fall of a royal family. Occasionally, foreign ethnic groups relied on force to enter and rule China, but they were eventually assimilated by Chinese culture. Once their military power declined, they collapsed and were overthrown. To seek a background that is complex, an organization that is strict, a foreign power like Soviet Russia as its external force, and the communism of Stalin as its ideal, and to destroy the military, political, and social organization of China in one fell swoop, like today's Red Peril, is truly unprecedented. This is especially something we cannot ignore.

The Xinhai Revolution advanced from a racial revolution to a political revolution, aiming to eliminate the deeply rooted patriarchal society and the thoughts and institutions of feudal forces that had existed for thousands of years. This could not be accomplished overnight. The republican system under the rule of the Northern Warlords was still doubted by scholars and celebrities, let alone a higher political ideal. The Three Principles of the People began to be noticed by the Chinese people after the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army in the fifteenth year of the Republic, but it still needs to be realized in the future to be deeply rooted among the people and manifested in facts. A nation must have a basis for its existence. Since the establishment of the Republic of China more than ten years ago, there has been no definitive highest political principle. The people have no firm political beliefs, and the result is today's anomalous society that is neither ancient nor modern, neither monarchical nor democratic. All economic organizations, moral concepts, and educational systems have followed it into a state of disintegration and collapse. In reality, today's China only has two paths: either to enter the Stalinist communism of plunder and slaughter, or to strive for the peaceful construction of the Three Principles of the People.

The development of the Red Peril can be divided into three stages. The first stage, from 1920 to 1923, can be said to be the period of utilizing the New Culture Movement. Chen Duxiu, Li Dazhao, and others received the mission and funding from the Third International and progressed from editing and publishing the "New Youth" magazine to running the "Guide Weekly," using the New Culture Movement to instill Soviet Russian communist ideas. Their achievements were more focused on society and neglected politics. The Third International嫌其迂緩 (was unsatisfied with their slow progress). At that time, the Chinese Kuomintang actually held the leadership of China's political revolution. The Third International then ordered Chinese Communist Party members to join the Kuomintang, which led to Joffe's visit to China and the reorganization of the Chinese Kuomintang. The second stage, from the Kuomintang's reorganization and acceptance of the Communists in 1924 to the Kuomintang's anti-communism in 1927, can be said to be the period of stealing the Kuomintang's party power. Borodin secretly held great power as a guest minister. The Kuomintang party departments at all levels, the political departments of various armies, and local mass organizations gradually came under the control of the Communists. At the same time, they carried out their so-called policy of dividing the Kuomintang by sowing discord and alienating people. The Kuomintang, unable to tolerate it any longer, subsequently saw the Nanjing-Hankou government turn against communism in 1927. The third stage, from the Kuomintang's anti-communism to the present, can be said to be the period of armed rebellion. In July 1927, He Long and Ye Ting rebelled in Nanchang. In December 1927, the Guangzhou communist riots. In July 1930, the Changsha communist riots were the most brutal and conspicuous of the major uprisings. From 1927 to 1931, the small-scale uprisings suffered by the cities and villages of Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan provinces were too numerous to count. In Jiangxi, a total of 81 counties were affected. At the height of the Red Peril (according to a report at the end of 1930), 32 counties and one city were completely under communist control, 22 counties and one city were partially under communist control, and there were 20 counties where the bandits had not been cleared. In Hubei, more than 50 of the 69 counties had been harassed by bandits. In southern Hunan, about ten counties had been harassed by bandits. Anhui, Sichuan, Fujian, Zhejiang, Henan, and Shandong also occasionally discovered traces of bandits. As for the results of their killing and burning, in Jiangxi province alone, more than 200,000 people were killed, more than 100,000 houses were burned, and the property loss was about 650 million yuan. In Hunan province alone, more than 70,000 people were killed, about 50,000 houses were burned, and the property loss was more than 15 million yuan. The number of people who died due to war and displacement and the loss of property are not included. The achievements of their uprisings and the speed of their spread are also alarming. As for the development of their forces, it is almost always related to internal wars. The Zhang-Huang War of 1927 was followed by the Guangzhou communist riots. The Zhang-Gui War of 1930 was followed by the Changsha communist riots. Last year, because the central military forces were concentrated in the north to suppress Yan and Feng, the Red bandits were able to calmly trample on the provinces of Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan, expand their military strength, and occupy local areas. Therefore, to thoroughly suppress the Red bandits, efforts should be made to avoid internal wars.

The Party-Government-Military Organization of the Communist Party: After the Kuomintang's anti-communism in 1927, the Chinese Communist Party split into two major factions: the Stalinist faction and the Trotskyist faction. The Stalinist faction absolutely obeys the orders of the Soviet Russian Communist Central Committee and is a loyal believer in Stalin. It advocates (1) armed rebellion to establish a Soviet regime; (2) uniting with intellectuals, middle peasants, and small merchants (i.e., the petty bourgeoisie) to overthrow imperialism; and (3) transitioning from a worker-peasant dictatorship to a proletarian dictatorship. Its central figures are Qu Qiubai, Zhang Guotao, and Red Army leaders such as Zhu De and Mao Zedong. The uprisings in Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan are all under the guidance of this faction. The Trotskyist faction supports Trotsky and the central cadres of Soviet Russia. It advocates (1) convening a national assembly to unite the masses and seize power; (2) seizing power with the proletariat to lead all classes and overthrow imperialism; and (3) the proletariat guiding and supervising the peasants to directly build a proletarian dictatorship. Its central figures are Chen Duxiu and others. The Stalinist faction calls this faction the liquidationist faction, saying that its advocacy of convening a national assembly is to eliminate class struggle. The Chinese Communist Party, which now holds real power, of course belongs to the Stalinist faction. Its party organization has established a central bureau in the Soviet Central District (this central district is currently in Jiangxi) to directly guide the special committees of the party in various Soviet areas. The special committees that have been established are the Xiang-E-Gan, Gan-Southwest (within the Central District), E-North, E-Yu-Wan, Gan-Northeast, Min-Yue-Gan, Guangxi Youjiang, and E-Xiang Border. Under the special committees are the district committees, which govern the county committees. Under the county committees are the city-district-township committees.

The Governmental Organization of the Communist Party: The highest organ is the Central Executive Committee of the Provisional Government of the Chinese Soviet Republic. Under it are the Xiang-E-Gan, Gan-Southwest (jointly called the Central District), Gan-Northeast, Yue-Gan, E-Yu-Wan, Xiang-E Border, Guangxi Youjiang, and Nanhai Island. The Soviet governments of the eight special districts. The special districts are equivalent to provinces and regions. Under the special districts are temporarily established county or independent city Soviet governments, which are directly managed by the special district Soviet governments. Under the county Soviet governments are the Soviet governments of various cities and townships. (To be continued)

Important News

Stationed in Shenyang

Japanese Consul-General Visits Zhang in Jilin

Informal Contact Regarding the Wanbaoshan Incident

Japanese Consul-General Agrees to Telegraphically Withdraw Japanese Police and Summon Zhong Yushi to Shenyang to Discuss

Shenyang Dispatch: After returning from Tokyo to take office, the Consul-General of Japan stationed in Shenyang, Hisajiro Hayashi, visited Zhang Zuoxiang's private residence at 10:00 a.m. on the 15th to express his condolences for the passing of Zhang's father. He then conveyed the wishes of Foreign Minister Kijuro Shidehara to China, saying that although the cabinet had changed, Japan's foreign policy towards China would not change. As for the Korean incident, it was a misunderstanding, and he hoped that it would not be amplified. He then clarified that he was informally discussing the Wanbaoshan case. Zhang Zuoxiang replied that because the Wan case had caused a major anti-Chinese incident in Korea, the Wan case could not be resolved locally at this time, but it would not be impossible if the Japanese side was willing to conduct preliminary negotiations locally. After obtaining the results, he would definitely ask for instructions from the Central Government. The first step should be for the Japanese side to telegraphically withdraw the Japanese police. Consul-General Hayashi accepted and immediately telegraphed to withdraw. It was then agreed that Zhong Yu, the special commissioner of Jilin, and Ishisha, the Japanese consul in Changchun, would come to Shenyang immediately to discuss a solution. Zhang Zuoxiang immediately sent an urgent telegram to the Jilin Provincial Government, ordering Special Commissioner Zhong to come to Shenyang as soon as possible. Japanese Consul-General Hayashi also telegraphed Ishisha to come immediately so that they could meet for discussions. (July 15)

Citizens of Harbin

Assist in the Wanbaoshan Case

City Chamber of Commerce Issues a Circular Telegram

Various Organizations Hold a Joint Meeting

Harbin Dispatch: The Japanese police who invaded Majiashaokou are still entrenched there and have forced the Koreans to restore the waterways in the three districts since the 12th, which has greatly angered our farmers. When Zhou Yubing, the director of the municipal preparatory office, heard about this, he sent personnel to persuade them to wait for official negotiations. Thus, the second conflict was prevented from occurring. The Kwantung Governor of Japan awarded 300 yuan to the Japanese police stationed in Majiashaokou for their hard work and sent a telegram to commend them, so the Japanese police became even more arrogant. On the 11th of this month, the Japanese consulate transported three large carts of luggage and bullets for full equipment, so under this kind of situation, local negotiations have become impossible. The Changchun Civic Diplomacy Association believes that the case could have been resolved at the beginning, but Lu Qi, the director of the county public security bureau, was timid and procrastinated, which led to such a serious situation, so it telegraphed the provincial government to dismiss and investigate him. Regarding the negotiations on this case, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently stated that the diplomatic commissioner Zhong Yu, specially appointed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of Harbin, would negotiate. When inquiring at the office of the diplomatic commissioner, it was said that no formal order had been received. Even if an order was received, negotiations in Jilin and Harbin were still uncertain, because the location of the incident was in Changchun. Since Changchun could not negotiate, negotiations would have to be held in Jilin. It is not yet certain whether the Japanese side will send Jilin Consul Ishisha to be responsible. Zhong Yu has not yet obtained the details of the cause of the case and the previous negotiations and has already telegraphed the Changchun Municipal Preparatory Office yesterday to transfer the entire case file to Harbin for preliminary reference and preparation. All circles in Harbin are extremely angry about the Wanbaoshan case and the massacre of overseas Chinese in Korea. The City Chamber of Commerce first issued a telegram to the central and northeastern authorities yesterday, requesting serious negotiations and expressing its willingness to be a supporter. The citizens have established the Harbin National Diplomacy Support Association for the Wanbaoshan Case and issued two declarations. The texts of the telegrams are recorded below: (A) To all compatriots in agriculture, industry, commerce, education, military, and police: Our country is in the position of a semi-colony, living under the iron hooves of various imperialists, and almost every day we are suffering from their trampling. The Northeast, because of its geographical location, has long been coveted by the insidious and vicious Japanese. In recent decades, because our country has swallowed its anger, the aggression of Japanese imperialism has become increasingly urgent, creating countless tragic events. At the same time, the Japanese forces in our Northeast are forming deep-rooted shapes, using resources to realize their so-called Manchurian centralism. In recent years, they have intensified their efforts and become more aggressive. The four railway proposals are enough to put us to death, and the occurrence of the Wanbaoshan Incident and the killing of overseas Chinese in Korea are the starting points for their pretext to seek opportunities to realize Manchurian centralism. It should not be regarded as a trivial matter. It is foreseeable that the great mountains and rivers will fall into the hands of foreigners, and our people will be destroyed and our families will be destroyed in an instant. The compatriots in important cities such as Changchun, Shanghai, Beiping, Liaoning, Tianjin, and other important cities have successively risen up to support and act as the backing of our country's diplomacy. Our Harbin City, as the key hub of the Northeast, is so silent and sits idly by while compatriots are brutally murdered, and willingly accepts the cold-blooded sarcasm of foreign countries, which is really heartbreaking. The colleagues of our association, as Chinese citizens of Harbin, have not yet cooled their blood and still have breath. We respectfully open our hearts and call out first. We think that all compatriots will be able to rise up and respond. If you do not forget the motherland and regard yourself as Chinese, please quickly unite with various circles to organize a support association for railway, Wanbaoshan, and Korean atrocities, etc., to fulfill the duties of citizens and benefit our country's diplomacy. At that time, our association will wholeheartedly help. Please unite together to do what we should do. The people unite together to implement national revolutionary diplomacy against Japan. Weak and small nations unite to overthrow imperialism and vow not to stop until the goal is achieved. (B) To the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Liaoning Northeast Political Affairs Committee: In Changchun Wanbaoshan, unscrupulous Koreans destroyed our farmland. The truth is that there is nothing to be heard. Even if the Koreans are foolish and stubborn, how can they not know the truth? Why do they stir up trouble and overflow at once? Cities in that country have successively evolved into the massacre of overseas Chinese. The reed houses are in ashes, and the corpses are littered everywhere. The tragic situation makes those who hear about it weep. If there is no one behind them instigating them, the Koreans would never be so unscrupulous. They are using the opportunity to test and seek to achieve great desires in our country. The instigators have other intentions. If we still adhere to the ancient訓 (teaching) of forbearance for the sake of the country, will there be any end to the trampling of imperialists' iron hooves? At the time of composing the owl, one cannot help but shudder. We humbly ask you to be mindful of the survival of the nation. This is the key. Quickly make serious protests, punish the brutal, and comfort the injured, and ensure that no such unfortunate events will occur in the future. Otherwise, how can our divine Chinese descendants be willing to become slaves? Work together and vow to avenge this humiliation. If the government promotes it from above, the people will naturally respond from below. Even though merchants are weak, they should also rise up and fight together. Urgent petitions are made to express the feelings of the subject. Harbin City Chamber of Commerce 元(Respectfully) (July 14)

Japanese Immigration Plan

Before the Wanbaoshan Incident Occurred

Using Agricultural Development as a Starting Point

Over 2,250,000 Mu Have Been Acquired

Shenyang Dispatch: The fact that the Wanbaoshan incident, a minor matter in a corner, has brewed into a fierce anti-Chinese movement among the entire Korean people is not without reason. Japan's policy of aggression against Manchuria has always been supported by political and economic policies. In the late Qing Dynasty, its economic policy was limited to commerce. After the early Republic, it increased its use of industry, and after the European War, it paid more attention to agriculture. It felt pressured by the excessive population in its country and feared the lack of food, so it thought of Manchuria's vast area and fertile land, which were suitable for large-scale agriculture, and thus actively engaged in operations. However, because the right of inland business lease in Manchuria had not been recognized by the Northeast authorities, it was an obstacle to its immigration policy. Therefore, it first transferred the surplus population in its country to the leased territories of Lushun and Dalian and the areas attached to the South Manchuria Railway, making them pioneers in agricultural development. Years ago, the Dalian Agricultural Association was first established, funded by the South Manchuria Railway Company with 5 million yuan. It first purchased land owned by the people in places such as Pi Zi Wo and Pu Lan Dian by means of high-pressure coercion, and also set up agricultural training institutes in Changchun, Gongzhuling, and Xiong Yuecheng to train specialized talents in farming and cultivation for the purpose of nearby materials. Subsequently, the East Asia Encouragement Company was established in Shenyang with a registered capital of 20 million yuan and a paid-up capital of 5 million yuan. It purchased approximately 124,672 町步 (cho) of land in the three northeastern provinces, with 1,297 町步 (cho) of paddy fields and 6,440 町步 (cho) of dry land under actual cultivation. The number of lands purchased in the three northeastern provinces in the name of Japanese private individuals or organizations is also more than 2,259,000 mu. As for the land occupied in the name of Chinese or in the name of Sino-Japanese joint ventures, or in the name of mortgage leases, it is even more numerous. The following is a list of land purchased by Japan in the eastern provinces (excluding the leased territory of Guandong 表州 and the land occupied by the South Manchuria Railway):

Purchaser Acres Location

Nangong Fangjiro 1111 Yingkou Tutaizi, Gaiping Sankuaishi, Tieling Fanjiatun, Shenyang Wujiahuang, etc.

Katsuhire Sadatsujiro 1060 Panshan Dingjiabao, Xinmin Muyuanzi, Shenyang Jing'anbao

Haraguchi Tontaro 389 Xinmin Gongtaibaotzu

Hisashi 143 Xinmin Sunjiatao

Sasa Ki 300 Fuxin Jujiangpaozi

Daire Shuji 820 Shuangshan Yamentun

The above are purchased with railway funds and the total value is over 300,000 yuan.

Jizai Maru 680 Tongliao

Mongolian Industrial Company 20013 Linxi area

Other 675000 (mu) Dagushan, Faku and other places

A total of 140,000 町, equivalent to our country's 2,259,000 mu. Last year, Japan established the Ministry of Colonial Affairs. After Minister of Colonial Affairs Genji Matsuda inspected Manchuria and Korea, he convened a meeting on colonial affairs to unify the policies of Manchuria and Mongolia, especially focusing on Manchuria's agriculture. In his speech, he said that he would use the full power of colonial affairs to increase immigration and that Manchuria was waiting to be developed. He encouraged everyone to work hard to develop Manchuria's natural resources. From this, he proceeded with his plan to immigrate one million people to the Northeast in 20 years, so as to make Manchuria and Korea one and incorporate our Northeast into its territory. According to a survey at the end of last year, the number of Japanese residing in the hinterland of the Northeast (Lushun) 10470 (Shenyang) 19103 (Kaiyuan) 2790 (Gongzhuling) 2032 (Fushun) 15317 (Andong) 2376 (Gaiping) 52 (Fengcheng) 16 (Hailong) 54 (Longjing Village) 961 (Kaiyuan City) 28 (Jilin) 930 (Taonan) 39 (Jinzhou) 103 (Harbin) 3366 (Dalian) 82682 (Pulandian) 936 (Dashiqiao) 2914 (Anshan) 594 (Liaoyang) 5028 (Tieling) 2780 (Sipingjie) 3326 (Changchun) 9440 (Benxi) 2538 (Fuxing) 3038 (Haicheng) 33 (Xingjing) 14 (Xinbin) 14 (Liuhe) 17 (Changtu) 37 (Zhengjiatun) 70 (Tongliao) 30 (Xinmin) 57 (Faku) 13 (Manzhouli) 176 (Jinzhou) 1312 (Piziwo) 954 (Yingkou) 2274. Statistics show that the above number is more than 181,200 people. However, this is only the number that is known. The number of Japanese and Koreans scattered in other places is estimated to be more than 2 million, with about 1.5 to 1.6 million engaged in agriculture. Because Korea has been our country's dependency for thousands of years and we sympathize with its tragic state of national subjugation, our country has allowed those who come to Manchuria to live in the hinterland as equals. This is enough to show the magnitude of our country's generosity. Who knew that it was falling into the trap of the Japanese? Because Japan has not obtained the rights of business lease in Manchuria, it is using Koreans to spread them throughout Manchuria and using a small number of Japanese to supervise and direct them to invade our agriculture and steal our land rights in preparation for negotiating inland residence and business lease rights. In recent years, there have been many tragic cases of Chinese farmers losing their lives and property, and although our authorities have negotiated with reason, the Japanese have ignored them. It is not difficult to prove the Japanese people's careful plans. Years ago, there were disputes over Japanese people invading and occupying the land of eastern provinces: (1) The East Asia Encouragement Co., Ltd. directed Japanese police to shoot and kill Chinese farmers in Xinmin County because of the purchase of land; (2) Japanese Feilong Tianqiang seized 7 Gongtai paddy fields and led police to shoot and kill the leader Han Xigui; (3) Japanese Sakakibara invaded the land outside the Beiling leased farm, first invading official land and then invading private land. In addition to these three cases, others are difficult to enumerate. On the one hand, 72 fortresses were built along the line of northern Manchuria last year, and this year, barracks are being built in Tieling, and the division stationed in Manchuria has been increased to two divisions. The defense police have also suddenly increased in number. Trenches have also been dug in Dalian and Lushun in mid-May, as if facing a great enemy. We did not know their intentions at first, but before we could turn around, the Wanbaoshan case arose. The clues cannot but make people deeply fearful.

The Fierce Battle to Suppress the Red Army and Capture Guangchang

Nancheng Headquarters Announces Victory by Telegram

The Remnants of the Red Bandits Plan to Flee to Fujian and Guangdong

Nanchang Correspondence: The recovery of Guangchang by the Suppressing Red Army was already reported in yesterday's news. Yesterday, the Headquarters received another victory telegram from the Nancheng General Commander's Headquarters, which is excerpted as follows: (1) According to a telegram from Chief Commander Zhu Shaoliang, our troops engaged in fierce battles with the Huang Gonglue and other units of the Red Bandits in the Ganzhuxu and Xiangjiacun areas for two days and nights. Our army occupied Guangchang city at noon, and the bandit forces, unable to withstand the attack, fled in the direction of Ningdu, etc. (2) Army Commander Chen's telegram at noon stated that our army engaged in a day and night of fierce battle with the main forces of Zhu De's bandit troops, Luo Binghui and Lin Biao, near Wenhui in eastern Guangchang. More than 4,000 rifles were seized, and the bandits collapsed in the direction of Baisha. We are currently pursuing them, etc. (3) According to a telegram from Army Commander Wei Hai, the entire Peng Dehuai bandit force, which had originally been in the Kangdu area and had sneaked from Jianning to harass our rear, engaged in fierce battles from dawn on the 11th until the evening of the 12th, stubbornly resisting in an attempt to make a final stand. However, our troops at Shizui, who had come from afar, encircled and suppressed them, completely annihilating the Peng bandit force, capturing countless prisoners, disbanding more than 10,000 coerced followers, and rescuing more than 600 men, women, and children who had been held for ransom. Among the bandits, Peng's forces were the largest among Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang. Now that Peng's bandit force has been completely annihilated by our army, it will not be difficult to pacify the remaining small bands in the near future, etc. After the recovery of Guangchang, there were intense battles near Donggu and its surrounding areas, such as Tantou, Langkeng, Shima, Shaxi, and Daijiafang. According to an airplane report yesterday, the area more than ten miles west of Longgang was ablaze with fire on the 13th of this month. It was said that the retreating Red bandits were burning their nests. According to another airplane report, Red bandits carrying stretchers were discovered in the area south of Ningdu, stretching for several miles. It is said that the Red bandits have indeed abandoned their old nests and retreated into Fujian and Guangdong. (July 17th)

He Jian Telephones Nanjing Urging for Funds

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province's military expenses are severely short and heavily in arrears. In addition, in the past two or three months, salt tax revenues have been low, and special taxes have been weak. The 200,000 yuan per month allocated by the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters for bandit suppression and miscellaneous expenses, and the 100,000 yuan per month approved by the Headquarters for Division Commander Wu's request, have not been remitted for two months, resulting in a severe shortage of supplies. Yesterday, in addition to telephoning General Commander Chiang and Minister Song to request 600,000 yuan to alleviate the urgent need, He Jian also specifically telegraphed Minister Song on the 7th, requesting that all the funds approved by General Commander Chiang be promptly allocated. The original telegram reads: [Strictly urgent, limited to two hours to Song Ziwen, Minister of Finance, Nanjing: I have received your secret telegram. After investigation, the military expenses of our army are severely short and heavily in arrears, and the situation is precarious. I have already exhausted all my words in Nanjing, and I hope for your understanding. Subsequently, I received the General's allocation of 500,000 yuan, which was only enough to clear one month's arrears. Not only is the situation as dire as before, but also because the current salt tax revenues are low and special taxes are weak, the income for May, June, and July is less than 400,000 yuan, resulting in a severe shortage of supplies and extreme hunger and fatigue. Previously, I received the General's telegram ordering Minister He to transfer 200,000 yuan per month from the special tax item for bandit suppression and miscellaneous expenses, and I received the General's reply to Division Commander Wu's telegram approving the monthly allocation of 100,000 yuan. Both cases were forwarded immediately after receiving the telegrams and have been urged repeatedly, with frequent urgent requests. Yet you, my brother, remain indifferent, not only not issuing a single penny, but not even replying with a single word. How can my efforts to reach the capital be successful? This is truly what I am deeply perplexed and cannot understand. Previously, I repeatedly received the General's order to open up岳郴寶 airport. At this time, the coffers of the tax collection agencies in Hunan Province are empty, with nothing to allocate. Only customs duties can be used. Therefore, I respectfully telegraphed to consult you. You rejected it on the grounds of not undermining financial unity. However, the customs duties are remitted to your department for redistribution. The use of funds is the same, whether before or after remittance, it is still under the allocation and order of your department, only the degree of urgency is different. It cannot be regarded as a defiance and resistance to financial unity. This is also what I cannot refrain from saying. At this time of intense suppression and military deployment on all sides, the perilous situation of having no pay and no provisions can be imagined. Yesterday, I specially telegraphed the General and you, my brother, requesting that 600,000 yuan be issued to alleviate the urgent need. I look forward to your consideration of our common plight and promptly allocate the previous funds to resolve the crisis and benefit the military situation. I eagerly hope and await your reply. Your brother, He Jian, bows. (Seal) (July 11th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Complete Crackdown on Kidnapping in Xiaokunshan: A series of kidnapping cases occurred in Xiaokunshan Township, the ninth district under the jurisdiction of the county, last month, causing extreme panic among the villagers. The police force in the district was also very weak. The district chief reported this and requested that a police team be sent to the township to investigate and make arrests. The Public Security Bureau dispatched inspector Yang Shijie to lead the police to the township for investigation. After nearly ten days, the criminals involved in the cases, Ruan Hucun (also known as Big-Foot Ah San), Zhou Xiaozhou, Xu Maonv, Wang Youyu, Yang Zixiang, and others, were apprehended and brought to the bureau yesterday. Director Shen, together with police chief Chen, interrogated them. According to the criminals, on the night of June 17, they kidnapped Gu Genbo and three others from Caobin, obtaining 500 yuan. Someone was in contact about the remaining 1,800 yuan to be paid in Xujiahui, Shanghai. They also kidnapped Pan Fengde's family in Xijinggang on the night of May 25. Seven accomplices went to kidnap them, and through someone's contact, they received 600 yuan. On the night of June 24, they went to kidnap Yu Hanzhang's family in Wangjiachang, Jin Hu, and later obtained a ransom of 700 yuan. They also kidnapped a family in Majiacun, whose name they did not know, and obtained a ransom of 400 yuan. They also obtained 400 yuan from Tao Songquan's family in Shijia Village. The victim in a certain family in Dapugang was injured and only 100 yuan was paid in Xujiahui. On the night of the 23rd of last month, they negotiated a ransom of 1,600 yuan for the kidnapping of Cao Wengao and Wu Yunqing's families in Tangcun Temple. About 25 ransom notes were delivered, and someone was sent to pick up the payment, but the victims were not at home. Only seven yuan was sent for travel expenses. After being treated to a meal, they returned to Shanghai and were arrested separately. Big-Foot Ah San has committed many crimes in Qingpu County. The decision to demolish the Dagang Pavilion: The Dagang Pavilion in front of the county government was designed by the former Director of the Construction Bureau, Xu, and its construction was approved by the county government meeting. After its completion, it occupied the streets and obstructed traffic. Merchants repeatedly petitioned for its demolition, but this was not allowed. The case was mentioned at the party and government talks the other day, and it was decided to demolish it. The news spread and the people were happy. It is now known that County Magistrate Shen has ordered the Construction Bureau to demolish it immediately based on the decision of the talks, and will also report it to the Department of Civil Affairs for record.

Suzhou

Three Soldiers Executed by Firing Squad: Regarding the Pingwang mutiny case, the Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters, in addition to transferring the two companies, the Second and Third Companies, of the First Battalion of the original garrisoned Xinzhen Fourth Regiment to the Suzhou North Hao Guild Hall for resettlement, and storing the 79 confiscated firearms in the headquarters, also dispatched the First Company of the First Battalion of the First Regiment, led by Battalion Commander Gao, to Pingwang for reinforcement. The seven principal culprits who were apprehended were interrogated thoroughly. According to their confession, they admitted that they had listened to the bandit line Lao Wei while stationed in Pingwang, and had made an appointment at the Pingwang Civilization Tea House to incite soldiers to go to Taihu to become bandits. Zhang Qindian (28 years old, from Shandong), Yan Caiming (19 years old, from Hunan), and Yin Ziqing (24 years old, from Hunan) were serving as squad leaders and were incited by bandits to incite soldiers. According to Articles 21 and 79 of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Criminal Law, they were sentenced to death. Zhou Jinbiao (24 years old, from Xuzhou) and Liu Fengming (26 years old, from Fujian) were deemed to be blindly following and were sentenced to eight years of imprisonment each. Zeng Qingbang (28 years old, from Hubei) and Shen Tinghua (29 years old, from Hunan) had not been in the army for long and their circumstances were lighter, so they were sentenced to five years of imprisonment each and sent to a military prison to serve their sentences. After serving their sentences, they will be sent back to their hometowns. Lao Wei and the soldiers who escaped are being wanted. Yesterday (the 18th) at 11:00 a.m., Li Mingyang, the Director of the Provincial Security Department, first gathered the stationed Suzhou companies near the ice factory outside Xumen for a speech, and then bound Zhang Qindian and the other two to Wangxiedun for execution by firing squad. Afterwards, Director Li sent 100 yuan each to the families of the three executed soldiers. Four More Lake Bandits Captured: Wang Wusheng, the captain of the eighth team of the Second District of the Dongshan Water Public Security Bureau, recently captured Zhang Zishui, a bandit involved in the consecutive kidnapping cases of Dongcuntou, Wuxiang, and Jianqiaotou. After questioning him thoroughly, yesterday (the 18th) he went to Zhang Zishui's home in Xiaodou, Ducun, and captured four more lake bandits and three fast rifles, and brought them to the Wuxi District Department for interrogation.

Wuxi

Court Begins Investigation into Murder Case: A male corpse with injuries was discovered in the Yangmuqiao River in the Second District (Jingyun City) last month. The county court sent personnel to examine the corpse and determined that the body had six stab wounds and had been murdered before being dumped into the river. The family of the deceased, Lu Zhang, identified the deceased as his son, Lu Rongquan, who was a plasterer by trade. Later, the mother learned that Lu Rongquan's death was due to a conspiracy by his mistress, Lu Yang, and her husband, Lu Asan, to kill him. She immediately filed a lawsuit with the county court, requesting the arrest of the murderers. After receiving the lawsuit, the prosecutor's office summoned the plaintiff to court yesterday to question her, ordered her to return home and await the arrest of the defendants for further investigation.

Prosecutor Appeals Lu Shiqiao Case: The prosecutor in charge of this case at the High Court, Jin Henian, believed that the judgment was inappropriate and submitted a written statement of reasons to the Supreme Court for appeal. The reasons he cited were: (1) The Criminal Procedure Law adopts the principle of direct trial as a fixed and unchanging principle. The fact that the defendant, Lu Shiqiao, participated in the conspiracy and incited Bao Dayuan and others to kill Tan Qixuan was unanimously confessed by the co-defendants Bao Dayuan, Lu Genhu, Guo Asi, and Zhu Ada in the Wuxi County Government, which also handled judicial matters. (2) According to the confession of the defendant Qian Fuyuan in another case (theft case): [I saw Bao Dayuan, Zeng Axing, Lu Shiqiao, and Lu Duanyi together in the Southeast Hotel on Xizang Road in Shanghai. I didn't know Lu Shiqiao, but Zeng Axing introduced us. I heard Bao Dayuan talking about how Lu Shiqiao and Tan Qixuan had a relationship due to their positions, and Lu Shiqiao used Bao Dayuan, Zeng Axing, Xu Bingsheng, and Lu Duanyi to shoot Tan Qixuan]. The above two points of directly obtained confessions were all discarded by the original judgment. Instead, the confessions of Guo Asi and Zhu Ada in the county government's records were adopted, which is inconsistent with the principles of criminal procedure. Furthermore, Qian Fuyuan is an important witness in this case. He was not confronted with Bao Dayuan, and it was not determined whether Lu Shiqiao and others were in the Southeast Hotel. The investigation of the duties was not exhausted, and therefore an appeal is filed for relief. Director of Finance Bureau Approved to Resign: Shen Ruji, the Director of the Finance Bureau of the county, has only been in office for one and a half months. Due to the county's depleted finances, the expected wheat harvest failed due to locusts, and the number of land tax collections was greatly reduced, making it difficult to cope. He repeatedly submitted his resignation to the Department of Finance, which was approved by the provincial government, and Wang Jingzhi, the Director of the Shanghai County Finance Bureau, was transferred to replace him.

Changshu

Party Committee Member Discovered Embezzling Funds: Shi Minbei, the current Supervisory Committee member of the County Party Headquarters in this county, is from Shazhou City in this county. He once served as a representative of the National Assembly in Jiangsu Province. It is said that Shi has been discovered to be embezzling funds in the name of the party, and the Haiyu Daily and Yuyang Daily have reported this in detail. The matter is roughly as follows: In the spring of the 17th year of the Republic of China, the Sangan River in Shazhou City was heavily silted, which was quite inconvenient for farmland irrigation. The gentry, Liu Bingshu, initiated the dredging of the river. The funds were collected from a special donation of two dimes per mu from the surrounding farmland, amounting to more than 2,000 yuan. After the river was dredged, villagers discovered that only half of the funds had been used, and Liu Bingshu was suspected of embezzlement. They went to the city to report to Shi Minbei. At the time, Shi was a member of the Party Committee, and he sent a letter to investigate and also sent a letter to Liu Jianbai, the head of the township administration (Jianbai was Liu Bingshu's nephew). The letter stated, [I have read the account and it has never been approved by the county government. It is completely privately collected national tax. I don't care if he subsidizes or compensates. I only know the compromise method. He (referring to Bingshu) takes out 500 yuan, or reduces it to 300 yuan, otherwise I will do what I can]. This was on July 12 of the 17th year. After Shi investigated, according to Liu Bingshu, the river funds were not enough and he had subsidized a lot himself, hence the statement. On July 17, Shi sent another letter to Liu Jianbai, saying, "The matter about your uncle has reached a stalemate. For the sake of brotherhood, I have offended your uncle, and I have approved the filing of a lawsuit with the judiciary." Then he said, "Please take care of your uncle's matter. If he is sensible, he will take out 500 yuan to settle the matter, or reduce it to 300 yuan for your sake, otherwise I will do what I can." Later, Jianbai sent a letter to his old friend Jianxin, saying that when his younger brother was in charge of local administration, he had used the black forces to extort 300 yuan from his uncle. The Haiyu Daily heard about this and published the whole story and the correspondence, and also took a film of the original letter. After Shi Minbei saw the newspaper, he issued a statement. A party member, Tong Shizhong, has filed a complaint with the county. Society is paying close attention to this matter. Bandits Plan to Rob the Suzhou-Changzhou Express Boat: After the river water rose sharply, all the boats at each port stopped sailing, so the Suzhou-Changzhou traffic was extremely isolated. Only a temporary number of fast private boats were used as an alternative for traffic. On the afternoon of the 15th, many fishing boats suddenly came to the Shenbang area of Guanghetang (ie the Suzhou-Changzhou route). They were very suspicious. The villagers questioned the men and women, but they were very evasive, and immediately got off the boat. The suspicion was even worse. The farmers rang the gongs and gathered the crowd to surround and detain three fishing boats. More than 200 chickens were found on the boats, and six bandits, men and women, were captured. After interrogation by the villagers, it was said that they planned to wait for the fast boat to pass by and rob it. The villagers tied the six bandits, men and women, to the trees on the river bank and announced to any ships passing by that they intended to rob the fast boat. Afterwards, the Public Security Bureau of the district heard the news and went to the spot to take the bandits to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Also, it was said that there were guns on the fishing boats, but when the villagers went to check, they were all sunk to the bottom of the river. It was also said that they had robbed a certain surname in Hengjing, etc. The Ransom for the Kidnapped Person in Nianbu Bridge is Paid: A kidnapping case occurred in Nianbu Bridge, Lao Wushi Township, Dongwu District, last year. When Lu Xincheng's grandson and four others were kidnapped, except for one person who was released to negotiate the ransom, the rest were still in the bandits' den. Lu Sunnian, 22 years old, received a letter from the bandits after his family was kidnapped, demanding a ransom of 20,000 yuan. Lu sold his family property and obtained 8,000 yuan, and then asked someone to contact the bandits in Chongming. After much begging, the bandits agreed to release the kidnapped person within three days. Lu Sun returned home the other day. He said that after paying the money, they tied his eyes and sent him to the seaside, forcing him to get on a fishing boat to Changjie. The fisherman asked Lu about the details and learned that he was a kidnapped person, so he sent him directly back home.

Jiangyin

Yangtze River Surveying Office Moves to Cheng: Jiangsu National Assembly representatives, in order to maintain the permanent prosperity of Shanghai, must first dredge the Yangtze River waterway. They have petitioned the National Government to send a team to conduct surveying in advance to serve as a basis for construction. It is now known that the Ministry of Communications has ordered the Yangtze River Surveying Team, which was originally located in the Hankou, Jiujiang, and Anqing areas, to move downstream for surveying starting in July. After receiving the order, Wang Yanfang, the captain of the team, sent Lin Youlong, the captain of the triangular team, to Jiangyin to start work at the old site of the North Outer Jiang Customs. All 120 personnel, including the team's members, clerks, and laborers, as well as four surveying vessels, have also arrived one after another and have been sent to designated locations to carry out surveying. The Situation of the Chengxi Road Being Washed Away by the Flood: Due to the disastrous continuous rain, the northern section of the Chengxi Road, from Jiejing Weiqiao to the Nanzha Canal Bridge, has been flooded, and most of the roadbed and bridges have been damaged. After the Construction Bureau sent technician Yang Jianxun to the countryside to investigate, it also sent a telegram on its behalf to the Construction Department for investigation. However, the road was originally scheduled to be fully open to traffic on the first of next month. In this case, it will have to be delayed again. Members of the Chamber of Commerce Collude with Bandits and are Arrested: Hou Youwang's family in Qiangjiaotou, east of Housheng Town, Second District, received 146 silver dollars the other day. They were robbed by six or seven bandits during the heavy rain. Afterwards, Youwang's son met a member of the Big Knife Society in Hejiazhuang (it is said that the Big Knife Society is very prosperous in Jiangyin, and many villagers have joined the society in the name of protecting their families). He told them that a bandit knew Hou. The Big Knife Society detained his cousin Hou Youzhang and Li Quanlin. They confessed that Yuan had initiated the plan and that Cao Weixin, a member of the Chamber of Commerce, had borrowed a box gun. After being taken to the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, Cao Weixin (ie Cao Weixin) was arrested in Yangku. On the 16th, he was taken to the county government. After being questioned by interrogator Wu, Cao and others confessed that they had been forced to become bandits by the bandit Li Jinchang, and that they had coerced accomplices to rob them. After interrogation, they were taken into custody.

Zhenjiang

Jiangsu Provincial Mining Exploration Area: The coal mine in Qinglong Mountain, Mantou Mountain, and Xiangshui Dam area of Jurong County, Jiangsu Province, has been investigated by the Department of Agriculture and Mining. The Ministry of Industry has approved it to be designated as a provincial mining exploration area. It is now reported that the Department of Agriculture has purchased drilling equipment and has identified the Xiangshui Dam coal mining area as the first drilling site to be tested. The department has appointed technician Zhang Yi to go to Longtan Town to make preparations. He has rented the house of Xietaiji Company in Hebei, Longtan Town, as an office.

Yangzhou

Dayuan Salt Company Expected to Resume Business: The Dayuan Company of Jinan in this city was closed down due to losses. It is now known that Mr. Feng Maoxuan has recently borrowed 250,000 yuan from a bank in Shanghai to come to Yangzhou to clear up previous debts and convene a shareholders' meeting to schedule the resumption of business. A Young Woman Commits Suicide by Poison: A woman surnamed Wang, a resident of Zhongxiaojie in the old city, was born out of wedlock and raised by her family. The woman is now of marriageable age. Suddenly, at dusk on the 15th, she ate her dinner, took a bath, changed her clothes, and went to bed quietly. Later, the family heard hiccups and found that she was in danger. Soon after, she died, and her skin showed a blue-purple color, as if she had been poisoned. She was put into a coffin on the 16th. It is said that the cause of death was due to rumors that her prospective husband's family thought she was unchaste and was about to cancel the marriage. The rumors reached the woman's ears, and she was indignant and committed suicide.

Nantong

Coastal Fishermen Claim Fishing Boats: Many fishing boats of the Lvsi Hechang fishermen were looted by sea bandits. Now that the bandits have fled north, the looted fishing boats have been abandoned. Fishermen Gu Huiren and others from various coastal ports have found the original boats and reported to the county government to claim them.

Jiaxing

Verdict in Xincheng Opium Case: The Jiaxing Xincheng Public Security Branch Bureau was found to have taken bribes from opium offenders and embezzled opium certificates. The local branch court discovered this and sent a letter to the County Public Security Bureau to place patrol officer Zhou Xingde of the branch bureau under surveillance and send him to the court for investigation. After summoning branch director Wang Maolie, clerk Ma Xiaoman, and patrol chief Yu Xiqi for interrogation, the court sentenced Zhou Xingde to more than one year of imprisonment. The others were acquitted. It is said that Zhou felt that the branch director should be responsible for the case and was unwilling to accept the verdict. He planned to appeal in the hope of getting rid of the crime. Wangjiangjing Wanchangcheng Rice Shop Reopens: The Jiaxing Wangjiangjing Town Wanchangcheng Rice Shop previously had a dispute with the head of the Third District Office, Pan Qinghua, who entered the shop to inspect opium. This caused the rice industry in the entire town to strike. After the local groups persuaded them, the rice shops resumed business, except for Wanchangcheng Rice Shop, which refused to resume business because of the huge loss. It is now known that the shop has filed a lawsuit with the court to resolve the matter. Therefore, the shop resumed business as usual yesterday.

Huzhou

Ling Guihua's Family Robbed and Owner Shot: Ling Guihua, a villager in Caohui, about ten miles outside the north gate of this city, was well-off. At about 12:00 midnight on the 15th, more than twenty bandits speaking with a Henan accent, each holding a wooden-cased gun and carrying a flashlight, suddenly came to his house and used stones to knock on the door. At that time, Guihua heard the alarm and knew that something was wrong. He immediately climbed onto the roof and threw tiles to repel the bandits. The bandits saw tiles flying down and shot at Cao, hitting him three times in the leg, causing him to fall to the roof. The bandits broke down the door and entered, searching extensively. They robbed more than one hundred silver dollars, several hundred taels of silkworm silk, and all clothing and soft goods. When the bandits left, they fired more than a dozen shots into the air and went towards Taihu. Afterwards, the family helped Ling Guihua down from the roof and sent him to the Wuxing Hospital in this city for treatment. Merchants and Residents of Changxing Petition for Postponement of Road Widening: On the afternoon of the 15th, more than 300 merchants and residents of Changxing County, under the jurisdiction of Huzhou, went to the Chamber of Commerce to hold a meeting and elected Li Peiying as the chairman. They said that the previous demolition of houses last year had caused losses to each shop and had not yet recovered. Moreover, Changxing's commerce was not prosperous. At this time of commercial difficulty, they wanted to widen the streets again. After discussing it for a long time, they decided to request the province to postpone the widening of the streets. The landlords elected Zhong Peicang and one other person, and the businessmen elected Li Peiying to go to the province to petition together.

Hangzhou

Series of Robberies on San Yuan Qiao Boats: Boats between Hangzhou and Yuhang County have been robbed several times this year. The other day (17th) at about 4:00 a.m., Wu Abing's boat from Xianlinbu and Meng Desheng and Gao Axian's boats from Yuhang were sailing towards Hangzhou. Just after passing San Yuan Qiao, six bandits suddenly came, and two bandits with guns ordered them to stop. They swarmed onto the boats and searched one by one. They robbed a total of about 300 yuan in cash and clothing. Afterwards, the three boat owners submitted a list of losses and requested the Hangzhou and Yu Military and Police authorities to investigate and arrest the bandits. Poppy Seedlings Everywhere, County Magistrate Receives Major Demerit: Yesterday, the Zhejiang Provincial Government approved a letter from the Provincial Executive Committee requesting an investigation into the widespread poppy seedlings in Jinyun County, as the county magistrate had not actively eradicated them. It was immediately verified by dispatching personnel that the county magistrate's handling of the poppy seedlings in his territory was indeed based on confidential reports from the people, and he only arrested and punished them after the fact. He did not actively investigate and eradicate them, and he also showed favoritism to the planting households. He has been given a major demerit as a warning.

Anqing

Li Chaoying Executed in Luan: During the Luan garrison mutiny in February of this year, Zu Songquan, the former chief of the Special Service Battalion of the Second Anhui Garrison Brigade, was executed by firing squad in Anqing on the 7th of the month by order of the Preparatory Army Corps Headquarters. Li Chaoying, the acting brigade commander of the Second Garrison Brigade, was also involved in the case. He had previously been detained in Luan. When Chen Diaoyuan went to Hefei and Luan to inspect the defense, he paid close attention to the case. According to a telegram from Luan yesterday, Chen had executed Li Chaoying by firing squad on the 15th to warn against lawlessness. Jin Youshu Approved to be Exempted from Custody: Jin Youshu, the former Director of the Anqing Municipal Preparatory Office, had been embezzling construction funds for the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall. The Provincial Government handed him over to the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau for custody for half a year. The Provincial Government's conversation meeting on the 17th decided that Jin Youshu should be exempted from custody and sent to the court for handling in another case.

Letter

Special Correspondent's Letter from the Dong-A Ilbo

To the esteemed editorial board: Your esteemed newspaper published on the 17th an item stating that Kim Lee-sam, a reporter for the Korean Dong-A Ilbo, was assassinated. This newspaper has no one by that name. Our Changchun special correspondent is surnamed Xu. This newspaper has never engaged in inflammatory propaganda regarding the Wanbaoshan Incident. We have consistently upheld the great principle of Sino-Korean mutual assistance and have strived to prevent riots. These facts are all documented. This statement is made specifically to clarify. Respectfully submitted, Shin Joon-yeon, Special Correspondent for the Dong-A Ilbo.

Letter from Lawyer Sun Zu-hong

To the esteemed editorial board: Having read a news item in your esteemed newspaper on the 18th regarding a divorce request by the daughter-in-law of the county magistrate of Wuxi, I must, on behalf of my client Gan Ran, make the following two points of clarification: (1) My client did not cohabit with Yang Bao-chun before their marriage in the winter of the 17th year [of the Republic]. (2) My client contracted syphilis from Yang Bao-chun and absolutely had no such disease before the marriage. I respectfully request that the above two points be corrected. Respectfully submitted, Lawyer Sun Zu-hong.
