Xu Qiuyue Accuses

Chen Jiongwen of Deceit and Abandonment

Demanding a One-Time Alimony of 120,000 Yuan

The woman Xu Qiuyue hired lawyers Dong Yu and Chen Zhigao to represent her in filing a criminal complaint in the French Concession court against her husband, Chen Jiongwen, for deceit and abandonment. The original complaint is recorded as follows: "For deceit, abandonment, and opium addiction, please prosecute according to the law and additionally file a civil suit requesting a judgment for alimony. The facts and reasons are stated separately as follows: (Facts) The plaintiff married the defendant as a concubine in May of the old calendar in the 12th year of the Republic of China. In the 13th year, the defendant's wife, Huang, passed away. He became addicted to opium and was confused all day long. The plaintiff advised him to no avail, and quarrels arose frequently. In April of the 16th year of the Republic of China, the defendant remarried Zhu as his successor. Zhu's nature was fierce, and she often gave the plaintiff the cold shoulder. The defendant also listened to Zhu's slander, and his treatment of the plaintiff gradually became alienated. There was constant scolding within the family. At that time, the defendant stated to the plaintiff that quarrels were inevitable between wives and concubines, and it would be better to live separately. In July of the same year, he accompanied the plaintiff to Shanghai, using the difficulty of finding a suitable house as an excuse to stay in a hotel temporarily. Little did she know that the defendant harbored malicious intentions to abandon her and secretly returned to his hometown residence without telling her. He never came back, and despite repeated letters urging him to come to Shanghai, he ignored her. The plaintiff's funds dwindled, and she had no choice but to move back to her mother's house. From then on, the defendant stopped caring about the plaintiff's life and no longer visited the plaintiff's mother's house. The plaintiff repeatedly sent letters but received no reply. She personally went to visit him several times, but he refused to let her in and then moved without a trace. The plaintiff has repeatedly suffered and is filled with remorse. The defendant used insidious tricks to deceive a weak woman, leaving the plaintiff with no means of support and no way to advance or retreat. (Reasons) The plaintiff and the defendant are husband and concubine, and in law, they are family members. The defendant has a duty to provide alimony. The plaintiff is now 24 years old and requires 200 yuan per month for living expenses. Calculating for 50 years, the defendant should pay the plaintiff 120,000 yuan in one lump sum. The defendant owns millions of dollars in property. The plaintiff's request is reasonable in law and in sentiment. Based on the above facts and reasons, the court is requested to consider that the plaintiff met the wrong person and is adrift without support. In addition to prosecuting the defendant according to the law, it is also requested that the court order the defendant to pay the plaintiff 120,000 yuan in alimony in one lump sum and bear the costs of this case." The defendant failed to appear after being summoned yesterday. The plaintiff's lawyer stated the circumstances. Judge Zhu ordered that the defendant be summoned again for questioning.

Wang Boqun and His New Wife Tour Putuo

Minister of Transportation Wang Boqun is scheduled to travel to Putuo next Saturday (i.e., the 25th of this month) with his new wife, Ms. Bao Zhining, to visit the scenic spots. He has already telegraphed the China Merchants Bureau to reserve the entire large dining room on the new Jianglun ship.

Huang Hanhou's Carving Exhibition is a Great Success

Huang Hanhou from Jiangdu is skilled at bamboo carving and adept at imitating calligraphy styles of various masters. Even on fan bones that are only a few minutes wide and less than a foot long, he can carve the "Chibi Fu," "Sacred Teaching Preface," Deng Shiru's long letter, etc., with characters as small as mosquito legs, yet the charm is exactly the same as the original. He is also skilled at carving teeth and reducing the entire calligraphy manual onto a two-inch insert, which is especially considered a masterpiece. Huang's marvelous skills have long been known throughout the country. Now, at the invitation of friends in the Shanghai business and academic circles and the art world, he has brought over a hundred recent works to Shanghai and is holding a public exhibition on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Fellow Association. Yesterday was the first day, and despite the scorching sun, the number of visitors was still endless. Everyone praised Huang's skills. It is heard that the exhibition period is only today and tomorrow.

Two Major Works by Zhou Shixun Published

Film Monthly and Star Biographies

Wenhua Fine Arts Picture Printing Company has recently been paying great attention to publishing periodicals in order to develop its business. In particular, the Film Monthly, edited by Zhou Shixun, is the most popular. Since its publication, readers at home and abroad have expressed satisfaction with the magazine's editorial content and printing. The ninth issue has now been printed and is scheduled to be published today. In addition to the original content, the current issue has been reformed and includes more pages of domestic film photos and news. The magazine is published monthly, costing 30 cents per issue. A full year's subscription costs 3 yuan and includes a free copy of the Star Biographies, edited by Zhou Shixun, which is also published today. In addition to exquisitely printed recent photos of major Chinese and Western stars, the book also contains 100 biographies detailing their origins, experiences, dimensions, weights, etc. It is the only publication of its kind in the domestic film industry in recent years.

Literary Star Weekly Publication Today

The first issue of Literary Star Weekly edited by Tang Zengyang has been published today. Main items include: Sun Chuangong's New Supplement for the Literary Scene, Tang Zengyang's Interview with Mr. Li Zanhua, Yang Changxi's Creation and Criticism of Remarque, Wen Juan's Brief Biography of Mr. Zhu Yingpeng, Zi Ping's Wang Duqing and Phonology, Shao Guanhua's Poetry, Zheng Fang's Novel Love, Hu Qian's World Literary Teatime, Zhang Ping's Recent Publication Review (three articles), as well as Chinese Literary Circle and Publishing Industry, Cultural Communication from Various Places, etc. The content is rich, and the writers are all well-known writers in China. It is an emerging literary publication that focuses on criticism of the literary scene at home and abroad and gives preferential treatment to those who pre-order. All those who pre-order a full year's subscription (52 issues) before the end of August will receive a 50% discount and will only be charged 7.5 cents. Subscriptions can be made at the Shanghai Modern Bookstore. All major bookstores also have distributors.

People's Livelihood Weekly Published Today

The People's Livelihood Weekly, which is dedicated to the study of people's livelihood issues, was published today. The content is rich, and the details of the negotiations between domestic manufacturers and the Municipal Council are accurately recorded. It also provides insights on the national economy and people's livelihood, as well as the recent anti-Chinese riots by Koreans. It is truly an outstanding publication in the modern era, and all our citizens should have a copy. In addition to those who hold the company's free coupon, who can directly claim it from the company, all newspaper vendors in this port have it for sale.

Giant Film Showing Again Today in Nanjing

Since Nanjing Grand Theater installed air conditioning, it has been showing excellent films. Today it will show another giant film, "The Scarlet Empress." According to reviews in Western newspapers and magazines, it is the most valuable achievement of Marlene Dietrich since her performance in the film "Resurrection." The entire film tells the story of a courtesan who, through her promiscuity and debauchery, causes her lover to be imprisoned, which in turn incites a prison revolt. As a result, police and prisoners fight each other, with casualties everywhere. Although the ending is happy, its sorrowful and poignant scenes move people to tears. The romantic depiction of the courtesan's life is particularly captivating. It is said that the theater will begin selling tickets at 9:00 AM this morning to avoid crowding.

Peide Company Sells Domestically Produced Mosquito Nets

Zhan Jicai, the manager of Peide Necktie Company, has recently manufactured a new type of domestically produced mosquito net. He hired specialized technicians to oversee the production, and the price is several times cheaper than imported goods. They are available for sale at 91 Sichuan Road.

Jiu Yu Tang Fan Exhibition

The owner of Jiu Yu Tang has collected over 300 pieces of calligraphy and painted fans from famous artists in Shanghai. The exhibition is being held at 51 Minguo Road, Xiaodongmen, for two weeks. Over the past two days, visitors have been very enthusiastic, with over two thousand people attending, mostly for appreciation. The works of Zhao Shuru, Ma Mengrong, Cheng Yaosheng, Zhang Shancun, Feng Chaoran, and others have already been completely sold out. Most of the other works have also been reserved. Ma Mengrong's two fans depicting crabs and flowers and plants are highly sought after by connoisseurs, and over ten pages of orders have been placed for similar paintings. Today, famous artists in Shanghai have been invited to the exhibition to create collaborative works on the spot, with temporary pricing for display to enhance the artistic atmosphere. In addition, new masterpieces by Ma Mengrong, Zhang Hongwei, Xie Gongzhan, Zheng Wuqing, Ma Gongyu, and others have been added. It is expected that the event will be even more lively during the holidays when people have more free time.

New Style Black "Puddle Jumper" Peerless Cars Arrive in Shanghai

The China Motor Company on Jing'an Temple Road has recently received several 1932 Peerless cars with rumble seats. The novelty of their design and the excellence of their mechanics are breathtaking. In order to give preferential treatment to all sectors, the Chinese General Manager, Mr. Zhou Mengxian, has decided to sell this first batch of cars arriving in Shanghai at the original price.

A property of over ten mu at the corner of Beijing Road and Xizang Road, including commercial buildings, with British title deed numbers 469 and 1246, and land registry numbers 575 and 576, has been purchased by the Dayao Construction Company's Real Estate Department for a price of 1,020,000 taels of silver. Also, an open space of approximately 46.7 mu bounded by Hart Road, Jiaozhou Road, Singapore Road, and Changping Road in the Western District, with British title deed number 12472 and land registry number 6098, valued at 780,000 taels of silver, has also been transacted by the same company. The owners who purchased the above properties all hold great expectations.

In yesterday's important announcement by Layman Zhengdao in the advertisement, the word "illness" [病] in "Zhengdao came to Shanghai to establish connections with sick families for several years" [證道來滬結緣病家數載] was mistakenly printed as "name" [名字]. Also, the character "Xian" [顯] in "Gengwu Jiaping Yehou Gao Shixian" [庚午嘉平野侯高時顯] was mistakenly printed as "Xuan" [軒]. This is hereby corrected. Special Announcement 6422

Ma Shang Hou North Branch Relocates

Ma Shang Hou Wine Shop has three branches in Shanghai. The main branch is in Maijiaquan, the South branch is in the old city at Nine Mu Di, and the North branch was formerly on the right side of Sanma Road and Shilu. Due to the renovation of all buildings near Sanma Road, the North branch has moved to a double-fronted shop across from the former site at the entrance of Xiejiangfang, and will reopen for business as usual today.

Lu Jintao Specializes in Song-Style Calligraphy

The Song typeface is elegant and beautiful. Since its promotion by the Zhonghua Book Company and others, it has become a fashion. However, the calligraphy is particularly difficult, so there are very few skilled practitioners. Mr. Lu Jintao, a calligrapher from Wujin, has studied this art for many years. His large and small Song-style characters are exquisitely detailed and have earned him a high reputation. Those seeking his work come in droves. Mr. Lu offers reasonable prices to establish connections through calligraphy and provide services to those who love beautiful Song-style characters. Submissions can be sent to the Fozhao Lou Hotel next to Donghexing Lane on Sima Road, and the Xie Wenyi Printing & Bookstore on Shandong Road.

Cao Zhenqing from the Civic Training Association and Sheng Yudu from the Social Affairs Bureau attended to provide guidance. Guests included Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce, and dozens of members. After the formalities, representatives from the higher-level organizations delivered speeches. Representatives from the Municipal Party Department, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended the meeting to supervise the election and provide guidance. Wu Yinhuai was publicly elected as chairman. After the formalities, the chairman reported on the progress of the preparations. The chairman gave a reply, and the meeting concluded with a group photo.

News from Various Labor Unions

Second District Knitting Industry Labor Union The fourth board meeting was held the day before yesterday, chaired by Zhang Zhuyun. Matters discussed included: (1) Jiang Bingnan raised the issue that the Da Shanghai Hosiery Factory had dismissed workers Zhong Shuqin and others without reason, and had requested assistance from higher authorities. The Social Affairs Bureau had summoned them for questioning twice but they did not appear. The resolution was to request the higher authorities to strictly handle the matter. (2) Zhang Zhuyun raised the issue that the Xin Ji Hosiery Factory was pressuring workers to join the union and refusing to register with the labor union, and had repeatedly done so, and had hired detectives to intimidate them. The resolution was to request the higher authorities to handle the matter according to law. (3) It was raised that the union's secretary, Zhou Weixin, had repeatedly requested to resign because he could not maintain his livelihood. The resolution was to provide him with a reasonable living allowance when the union's finances improved, and to unanimously retain him.

Second District Water and Electricity Industry Labor Union A meeting of representatives from various departments was held yesterday, with Zhang Renjun elected as chairman. He reported on the purpose of the meeting. Next, communications representatives Dong Guixiang and Zhu Along successively reported that they had requested Mr. Du Yuesheng to negotiate with the company to request the reinstatement of 27 workers. They had agreed to reply on Sunday. All the workers were satisfied and are waiting for a resolution.

Western Restaurant Industry Labor Union The fourth board meeting was held the day before yesterday, chaired by Yao Zhongqing. Matters discussed included: (1) Secret. (2) The seven labor-management conditions raised at the general meeting have been submitted to the competent authorities for approval. A resolution was passed to appoint Zhao Jinghua, Wu Shenxiang, and six other comrades as responsible representatives to negotiate with the employers. (3) A resolution was passed that the work procedures for the heads of each department of the union should be stipulated, and that each department director should stipulate the on-duty hours for each staff member, and that regular meetings should be convened once a week. (4) Comrade Wang Futing proposed how to deal with workers who have not joined the union. A resolution was passed to send the investigation department to investigate, and then send the publicity department to persuade them to join.

Toothbrush Industry Labor Union The eleventh meeting was held the day before yesterday, chaired by Liu Tazu. Matters reported included: (omitted). Matters discussed included: (1) The first branch office requested that Tao Xiaomei, Wu Sao, and Zhou Wenxiang be admitted to the union. After review, they were deemed qualified and approved for notification. (2) The fifth branch office submitted the following cases: A. Member Zhou Guihua was absent from small group meetings without leave. B. The Shuanglun Factory sometimes uses temporary workers to replace regular workers, hindering the prospects of the regular workers. C. Regarding wage issues. Resolutions were: A. Punish according to regulations. B. Investigate and if it is not true, C. Send a letter to the factory manager to arrange a date and location for the union to send representatives to discuss. (3) Who should be sent to attend the Shuanglun meeting? A temporary appointment was made. (4) Member Wang Dabao requested a travel allowance from the union because he was returning to his hometown due to illness. A travel allowance of five yuan was approved, with the remainder subsidized by Mr. Tian and Mr. Zhou. (5) Worker Ding Ruichun from the manufacturing industry repeatedly wrote letters begging the union for relief. The reply was that they would do their best to help when the opportunity arose. (6) Re-deliberation of the death benefit for deceased member Mei Qiyun. After investigation, the resolution was that Mei Qiyun's family was wealthy and the matter had passed, so it was not necessary, but a souvenir should be made to commemorate him. (7) The Liang Xinji Factory sent a letter requesting that the grinding department open night shifts for one month due to busy work. The resolution was to wait for the second branch office meeting before reviewing and first reply to the factory. (8) How to resolve the wage issue of the Liang Xinji grinding department? The decision was to convene a meeting of the entire second branch office this Friday, with supervisor Zhou, director Liu, director Dong, and secretary Qian attending to provide guidance. (9) How to deal with the third branch office's failure to submit dues for June? The resolution was to send Ouyang Changan from the general affairs department to question them. (10) The Second District Silk Weaving Industry Labor Union requested assistance because the Jin Xin Silk Factory dismissed workers. The resolution was to subsidize one yuan. (11) The preparations for the club have been completed. Should a founding meeting be convened? The resolution was to wait until registration is complete before deciding. (12) How should the workers' supplementary classes be conducted? The resolution was A. Enrollment dates from today until August 10th. B. School starts on August 20th. C. In addition to Secretary Qian, Mr. Tian Yuliang and other specially appointed lecturers will be hired. D. Each student will pay a deposit of one yuan, which will be forfeited if they are absent for more than three weeks. E. Supplies and books will be provided by the union; other items will be self-prepared. F. Courses include Chinese, general knowledge, arithmetic, and lectures. G. Time: 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM. (13) Member Zhong Ruisheng requested a loan for travel expenses because his father had passed away and he was returning to his hometown. The resolution was to temporarily loan him ten yuan by postal remittance.

First District Transportation Industry Labor Union Yesterday, workers from Changyuan Transportation Company, affiliated with the Fresh Pig Office, were obstructed and harassed while loading pigs onto barges. A general meeting of workers from various transportation companies was held to discuss how to deal with pig merchants soliciting customers and recruiting multiple transportation companies, hindering workers' livelihoods and depriving them of their inherent benefits. The entire meeting unanimously resolved: (1) To recover the agreed-upon five cents (plus two cents for Huai pigs) per pig for transportation and enjoy it themselves. (2) Regardless of the number of pigs or whether the merchants solicit customers themselves, all pig bills of lading must be handed over to the transportation company for loading and transportation (the company's water fee will be paid by the pig merchants soliciting customers themselves). (3) If there is any infringement, the benefits they should have received must still be collected from the employers as usual. (4) To implement this in its entirety on the 20th of this month, and send letters to the heads of various companies to follow suit and issue notices for public awareness. (5) The employers should be fully responsible in the event of a disturbance. All of the above was passed and the meeting adjourned.

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that it will be hot and cloudy along the coast, with possible thunderstorms in the Yangtze River basin. There will be southeast to southwest winds of varying strength in the East China Sea and the Yellow Sea. Educational News

Important News

Jiangsu Province

Middle School Requests Budget Increase

Call for Education Fee Committee Meeting If No Results

Schools province-wide will postpone reopening after the summer vacation.

Zhenjiang Communication On the morning of the 16th of this month, principals of provincial middle schools gathered at the Provincial Middle School. Principals and representatives from schools including Shangzhong, Yangzhong, Tongzhong, Zhenzhong, Taizhong, Huaianzhong, Songzhong, Aquatic Products School, Song Girls' Middle School, and Xu Girls' Middle School discussed and resolved six items: (1) What to do about the cancellation of the remaining funds for the 18th year's temporary expenses as decided by the Education Fee Committee? The resolution was to strongly oppose this decision. Two measures were adopted: (a) Send a representative to meet with Chairman Ye to request the immediate disbursement of the subsidy fees owed by the provincial government for both the 18th and 19th years in order to clear the temporary expenses for that year. (b) Submit a request to the Education Department to convene an Education Fee Committee meeting before August 5th to reconsider this matter, and at the same time send a direct letter to the Education Fee Committee detailing the reasons and requesting reconsideration to allow for the restoration of funds. (2) The amount of temporary fees for the 19th year allocated to each school by the Education Department is far from meeting the actual needs of the schools. What should be done? The resolution was to adopt two measures: (a) Explain to the Education Department that the distribution and announcement of the temporary fees for the 19th year was delayed until the end of the year, while schools had to make expenditures during the year to meet practical needs, resulting in significant discrepancies. Efforts must be made to provide relief. (b) Before mid-August, each school should submit to the Education Department the amount of temporary fees actually spent in the 19th year, along with receipts, for review and verification, and funds should be allocated accordingly. (3) How should the temporary fees for the 20th year be determined? The resolution was to request the Education Department to verify and announce the fees within two months after the start of the year to avoid repeating the difficulties encountered in the 19th year, where the amount was determined after the fact. (4) The budget for regular expenses for the 20th year also does not meet actual needs. What should be done? The resolution was to request the Education Department to resubmit the previous request to expand the regular expenses for the 20th year and to submit the proposal to the Education Fee Committee for review and approval at the Education Fee Committee meeting convened before August 5th, and to make every effort to increase the budget. (5) If the convening of the Education Fee Committee cannot be realized or if the meeting results still adhere to the original stance, what should be done? The resolution was to adopt four measures: (a) Beforehand, each principal should explain the actual difficulties faced by the schools to Director Chen, Chairman Ye, and Director Niu. (b) When necessary, make a public announcement detailing the aforementioned difficulties to society. (c) When necessary, publish a notice in the newspapers informing students that the start of the 20th year will be temporarily postponed. (d) Principals should resign immediately if the various funding shortages prevent the schools from being maintained or continued. (6) The phrase "examination results are satisfactory" on graduation certificates is too general and lacks effectiveness. How should it be improved? The resolution was to submit a request to the Education Department for approval to include the students' academic, conduct, and physical education grades for each semester on the back of the graduation certificate to acknowledge and encourage achievement.

Breathing a Sigh of Relief

The Eagle Team Forcefully Defeats Shangda

Thirty-Four to Twenty-Five

Referee Stands Up for the Country

Cannon Team Sends Out a Mighty Force Tonight

Last night was the second match for the Japanese Shangda Basketball Team in Shanghai. As a result, they lost to the Eagle Team by a score of 25 to 34. The Cannon Team will be in action tonight at 8:00 PM against the Japanese army, still in the basketball room.

Eagles Display Their Might The Eagle Team was superior in both form and technique last night. The Japanese army relied only on their strong physical strength. However, the Eagle Team also fought to the death to resist. Initially, the Eagle Team had an overwhelming advantage of nine to two. Shangda chased the score to ten to seven. The Eagle Team then won by a large margin of fifteen to seven. The first half ended with fifteen to thirteen in favor of the Eagles. In the second half, Shangda once chased the score to twenty-two to nineteen. Seeing this difficult situation, the Eagle Team unleashed their full power and launched a counterattack, finally winning by a large margin of thirty-four to twenty-five. The spectators were delighted.

Coach Participates Shangda's coach, Ueda, was a player from Liaodong, Japan. Seeing that Shangda had already lost, he joined the battle, trying to turn the tide. At one point, the score was twenty-nine to twenty-five with five minutes remaining. But in the end, nothing was gained, and his technique was mediocre. The Japanese army had no confidence in throwing the ball.

Using Chinese Shao Ji, the referee last night, used Chinese. Shangda protested and asked to use English, but he remained unmoved. In a competition in China, Chinese should be used. The Japanese had no choice but to accept it, which was quite a victory for the Chinese people.

Sponsored by China East Company

China Student Tennis Tournament

Fifteen University Athletes in Shanghai Participate to Compete

Forty-Four Singles Players to Compete Starting Tomorrow Two

Twelve Doubles Pairs to Begin the Day After Tomorrow

This China Student Shanghai Tennis Championship sponsored by the China East Sports Company has been reported in this newspaper. It is learned that registration closed at noon yesterday. Students from various schools joined enthusiastically, with 44 singles players and 22 doubles teams, truly opening a new era in the tennis world. The competition is scheduled to begin tomorrow and will be held every afternoon at 2:30 PM, ending in about three weeks. The competition list has been drawn by the committee according to the rules of the world tennis competition. Therefore, many people were not drawn into the first competition. The competition dates are stipulated in the rules, and there will be no postponements except in the event of rain. It is hoped that all contestants will pay attention. In addition to the finals and semi-finals being designated by the committee, the referees for the remaining competitions will be appointed by the consent of both parties as necessary. Please report the results of the competition on the same day to Zhou Jiaji of the Association for circulation and notification to the newspapers. It is also learned that new balls will be used for all of the competition, but after the competition, the China East Company is willing to sell them at half price, eight yuan per dozen and two yuan for every three, and can be contacted by the company. Davis Cup Interzone Final

Equal Strength Between England and America

Each Wins One Singles Match

Paris, 17th (electric dispatch) English and American players are today competing for the Davis Cup tennis championship here, with each winning one singles match, resulting in a draw. The doubles match will be held tomorrow.

First and Second Singles Results

2-6 Austin (Eng) 6-0 Wood (US)

8-6 7-5

10-8

Shields (US) 6-4 Baly (Eng)

Global Attention After Ten Years

It has been eleven years since England and America last competed in the Davis Cup, and it has been far away in 1920 when the United States eliminated England in the second week of the competition. This reunion has attracted global attention. The British believe that this year is the period of British revival with the strongest strength and the greatest hope. The American team's players are the youngest this year, and everyone is worried that they will not be able to win the competition.

Wimbledon Champion Loses

In today's first singles match, the American Wood, the Wimbledon champion, lost to the Englishman Austin. Wood's serve was very strong, but he lost three sets in a row. However, the competition was fierce, with the third set having a total of fourteen games and the fourth set twelve games. Austin's pressure balls were fierce and corner shots were accurate. Wood was busy coping with Austin's ever-changing strategy. In the second singles match, Shields defeated Baly easily without much effort.

America May Win the Doubles Match

With each side winning one singles match, the doubles match has not yet been decided, and two singles matches on the third day will be necessary. The American team, Van Lingle and Lord, are likely to win the doubles match.

French Spectators Greatly Worried

The French are paying close attention to the battle between England and America, but they are greatly worried that they may not be able to keep the Davis Cup this year. This is because the two teams in the Interzone Final are both very strong, and France may not be able to win. The finals will be held next week.

Municipal Bureau of Education Reports to the Education Department

Interim Standards for Secondary School Curriculum Experiment Results (I)

The Interim Standards for Primary and Secondary School Curriculum have been promulgated and implemented for experimentation by the Ministry of Education for over a year. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has established a Research Committee on Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools. Now, following the Ministry's order to report the results of the experiment, the Bureau will reconvene to discuss and compile a report based on the results of the experiments conducted by various primary and secondary schools in the city. In addition to the primary school section already published in the previous report, the full text of the secondary school section is recorded below:

Shanghai Municipal Experiment [Interim Standards for Secondary School Curriculum]

Result Report

Chinese Language

Second, Time Allocation

(I) The time allocated for intensive reading instruction in junior high school Chinese should be increased to four hours [Reason] According to the experimental results, the form of intensive reading and composition is relatively long and the content is relatively complex, so each unit cannot be completed within three hours. If it is shorter, three hours is a bit too long. Thus, each week's teaching materials are often divided. If one hour can be added, the longer and more complex ones can be completed within the week, and the shorter and simpler ones can be connected to two articles, which can also be completed within each week. Moreover, most of the textbooks applicable to each semester prescribed in the market have forty to fifty articles. On average, there should be intensive reading guidance for two articles per week, and the time is already insufficient. In addition, grammar and rhetoric instructions, questions, tests, dictation reports, discussions, and review of notes require even more time for grade assessment. It is difficult to take care of everything. Therefore, it seems that intensive reading guidance should be scheduled for four hours per week.

(II) It seems that one hour should be added to the junior high school calligraphy class within the Chinese language class [Reason] Practicing calligraphy outside of class provides no opportunity for on-site guidance, making it difficult for students to improve. It seems that one hour of calligraphy time should be added to the six hours per week for intensive reading, extensive reading guidance, and composition practice.

(III) High school Chinese composition should be assigned once a week, alternating between in-class and out-of-class assignments each week [Reason] According to page 14 (3) of the High School General Course Curriculum Standard, composition practice (1) assigned composition in the classroom can cultivate students' habits and abilities of quick writing. Out-of-class composition can cultivate students' habits of detailed writing and expressing their abilities as much as possible. Therefore, it seems that composition should be assigned once a week, alternating between in-class and out-of-class assignments each week.

Fourth, Teaching Material Outline

(I) The proportion of classical Chinese materials in each grade of junior high school Chinese teaching materials should be slightly increased [Reason] According to students' learning status, they seem to have a deeper impression of classical Chinese selections. In terms of recitation, classical Chinese is especially effective. Junior high school is the foundation for cultivating students' classical Chinese skills. If the amount of classical Chinese teaching materials is not reduced excessively, it is easier to get training opportunities.

English

Second, Homework Requirements

The procedure for ear, mouth, eye, and hand training in the high school English homework requirements column is well coordinated, but high school English should especially focus on eye and hand practice [Reason] High school English courses should focus on training reading and writing skills, so eye and hand practice is more important than ear and mouth training.

Third, Time Allocation

Junior high school English grammar and reading books should be taught separately [Reason] Mixed teaching of grammar and reading books is in line with learning principles, but the results of the trial implementation are not as good as separate teaching, which can be mutually confirmed and systematic. The five hours of English should be stipulated as three hours for reading books and two hours for grammar.

Fourth, Teaching Material Outline

(I) The content of the high school English teaching material outline is still rich, but English grammar for the first and second grades of the general high school should be included [Reason] If the first and second grades do not teach grammar separately, the foundation of sentence construction and composition will not be solid, and the rhetoric essentials of the third grade will be difficult to learn.

History

Second, Teaching Material Outline

(I) There are too many political historical materials [Reason] The function of history is to examine the past and understand the present, and to use the gains of past human life, academic thoughts, and ideas as a way to improve today's human life and social undertakings. However, according to the curriculum standards, it seems to focus too much on political historical materials of past dynasties, so it is appropriate to compress that historical material as much as possible and increase the historical material of people's livelihood and the historical material of academic thought. (II) The teaching material outline should be based on the objectives listed and take the Three Principles of the People as the central ideology [Reason] Although the history curriculum is inevitably based on a flat narrative of facts due to its timeliness, there should be a central ideology to connect all materials. For example, our country now uses the Three Principles of the People as the standard for pure people's thought, and the objective item of the curriculum standard also says that it aims to expound the historical origin of the Three Principles of the People. Therefore, the teaching material outline may as well use the origin or evolution of the Three Principles of the People as a central ideology, so that scholars have a purpose in learning, and historical materials will not be scattered and have nothing to return to.

(III) Too much emphasis is placed on the chronological system [Reason] The curriculum standards for national history and foreign history in high and junior high schools are all narrated in chronological order, so the comprehensive analysis method is not convenient to use, and most of the materials in ancient history are not convenient to connect with current affairs. It seems that the compilation of the chronological system should be broken, and various important activities in human life should be used as learning units.

(IV) Chinese and foreign history should be linked to each other [Reason] Chinese history and foreign history should be taught separately, but it is appropriate to link them when teaching, so that scholars can understand the characteristics of the history of various countries, use the comparative observation, analysis, and synthesis methods, and cultivate a world view. The teaching material outline seems to have not taken into account this aspect.

(V) Junior high school national history has always been taught from ancient times to modern times, but the results obtained from teaching seem to require reversal. If it is taught from modern times to ancient times, it will not only be more effective, but also avoid many difficulties in teaching [Reason] 1. Anyone who studies history admits that ancient times are more difficult than modern times. The further away from us the history is, the more difficult it is to study, because there are many things in ancient history that need to be distinguished between true and false, and we have to bring a little textual research. People who don't have much research on history feel the most difficult about textual research. This is the reason why ancient history is more difficult to read than modern history. Now, let the first-year students who have less research on history read the most difficult ancient history, and let the second-year students who have more learning on history read the easiest modern history. Such a reversal of difficulty will inevitably cause difficulties in teaching. 2. Anyone who studies history feels that the more ancient, the more boring it is, because ancient times are far away and it is not easy to evoke imagination, and it is difficult to understand the relationship with our current life. Modern history is like something that happened yesterday, and it is easy to evoke imagination and feel that it is related to ourselves. Now, putting boring ancient history to first-year students is like giving a head start to those who want to enter the hall of history. It will be difficult for them to develop an interest in studying history again. If modern history is used as the starting point, it can not only make students have a strong interest in history and work hard to explore, but also make students start to pay attention to current affairs, develop the habit of reading newspapers, and make students research layer by layer from modern to modern times, from modern times to the Middle Ages, from the Middle Ages to ancient times to explore the origin of the current situation and the source of today's major problems. 3. Distributing teaching materials and estimating time are the things that teachers should pay most attention to, but special holidays and other reasons often break the distribution and estimation, so that the last part is abandoned. Teaching history cannot be outside of this. It is often because there is not enough time that the most important modern history is abandoned. If modern history is used as the starting point, there will be no such concerns.

Free Talk

World News in Brief

—Hai Ke

British Club Movement

There are two famous British doctors, one of whom is a woman, who are planning a great thing to organize a health club throughout the country so that the working class of the whole country can get proper entertainment and benefit their physical and mental health. The club has facilities such as swimming pools, dance halls, card rooms, and other kinds of entertainment, as well as dining rooms and wine stalls to supply members with food and drink, but the wine is limited to beer because it is not easy to get drunk and is relatively beneficial. Each headquarters has 2,000 members, each family paying one shilling and a few pence per week to cover the cost of various physical exercises. The babies of each family can roam around in the club all day, and the children can go there after school. In the afternoon, it is specially for mothers to gather, and in the evening, parents can go together to seek a night of joy. They also have an advisory department for all kinds of trivial matters of the members to provide consultation. Whether old or young, married or unmarried, if they have any difficult problems to solve, they can go to discuss them. This is truly one of the most beneficial clubs in the world.

Children in the American Film Industry

Parents in the United States, seeing that children can earn a lot of money in the film industry, send their children to make movies. As a result, the number of child actors is increasing day by day. The local authorities, in order to ensure their safety, have strict restrictions on film companies. Each child must not work more than two hours a day, and must not be under strong lights for more than thirty seconds at a time.

Blind Donkey

—You Cen

The Blind Donkey is a heroic man in Baodu Mountain, Shandong Province, named Zhang Baishun. He is blind in one eye and has a very strong personality. Whenever there is a bandit alert, he immediately steps forward, carrying two guns to meet him, and carrying a food bag as a farmer trading to avoid bandit suspicion. He travels quickly over mountains and ridges. The name Blind Donkey comes from this.

Every time he fights with bandits, he often leads several people to attack their vitals or directly explore the bandit dens, so the bandits are in chaos without fighting. He then exerts his strength to capture and kill them. Those who stand in his way are overwhelmed. At night, his single eye is bright and his vision can reach several miles away. The bandits all warn each other not to offend him. There is also a saying that if you do evil at home, you will meet the Blind Donkey when you go out. The hundreds of villages in the south of the mountain rely on him for a peaceful life. His heroic spirit is like this.

What is most admirable is that after the bandits do not offend him, he actually sends a letter challenging them, agreeing on the date and place of the battle. Whether the bandits honor the agreement or not, he then deliberately sets up suspicious soldiers and robs the bandits' wives and children as conditions for ceding land and paying compensation, and all the proceeds are used to purchase guns and equipment for the militia, without taking a penny for himself.

This spring, the army jointly suppressed the Baodu Mountain bandits. The Blind Donkey was recruited by Guo, the commander of the 347th regiment of the 58th division of the army, and ordered to be a guide to explore caves and find nests. He was very helpful. I came to the mountains with the army and heard the name of the Blind Donkey several times. I am afraid that he will be buried and unknown, so I recorded his outline here to serve as a lesson for those who are willing to suffer from bandits and are timid and dare not resist. (No payment accepted)

Clever Response to Thank You Wine

—Jian Fan

Someone used Three-Star Brandy to thank Mr. Li Jinglan of Linchuan for his painting. It happened to be the season of Huangmei, and Mr. Li took the wine and listened to the rain, and his elegant interest was greatly developed. He came up with a clever idea and replied with a couplet "Three-Star Brandy" and "April Huangmei Day" to inscribe a long postscript to report it. It is exquisitely neat and seamless. (Payment returned)

Bee Matchmaker Flower

—Chi Fo

Recently, stories of free love and amorous affairs have been heard from time to time. Those who are dissolute should be criticized by the world. As for what I heard about Ms. K, her talent is like Xie Daoyun and her encounter is like Zhuo Wenjun, which should be discussed separately. Ms. K is from eastern Zhejiang. She is beautiful and intelligent, and has a innocent nature. At the age of nineteen, she graduated from a girls' middle school in Shanghai and married Mr. D from the same town. Mr. D is upright and ambitious. He first entered a certain higher school in Japan to study engineering, and then he thought that his hometown had many great Party-State figures, so he changed to a military academy. He got up at dawn to exercise his body and burned the midnight oil to study hard. He was overworked and suffered from stomach problems. After getting married, he went to the East again. Unfortunately, he died suddenly after less than a month. Ms. K cried bitterly when she heard the news. From then on, she lived a lonely life and spent her time teaching. There is a women's school in the town that specializes in accepting women who have dropped out of school and teaching them ordinary knowledge. The results are excellent and it is famous. Ms. K entered the women's school as a teacher, and the teachers and students have a very close relationship. It is probably because the women's world is dark and they deeply feel the same disease and pity each other. Once, Mr. S, a primary school teacher who studied beekeeping, was young, handsome, and romantic. He heard that Ms. K's hometown was a land of industry before it produced great people. Agriculture, mulberry, and animal husbandry have always been requested. The water honey peaches and big taro have long been famous and called specialties. In recent years, there have been many beekeeping and sericulture families. Mr. S heard that the women's school had a lot of Italian bees, so he came to visit. He suddenly saw Ms. K. During the conversation, the affection was lingering. A bee flew on Mr. S's lapel. Ms. K waved it away and it plunged into Ms. K's arms, buzzing and flapping its wings. Ms. K smiled at it. After that, the two often visited each other. Mr. S often revealed his intention to propose. Ms. K only laughed foolishly. Her heart was uneasy and she could not make up her mind, so she visited her friend and discussed it. The friend said to Ms. K: Women are not forbidden to remarry by law. Such a beautiful face is like flowing water, how can they waste it idly? Moreover, the ancients used red leaves as matchmakers and it has been passed down as a good story. Bees and butterflies are originally matchmakers for hundreds of flowers. Now they wave them away but they come again. Isn't it a match made in heaven? What's the suspicion? Ms. K's intention was decided. Now, a pair of Bi people plant flowers in several fields and raise bees in several rooms, wandering among the misty light and stream sounds to spend their honey-like time. I named this article "Bee Matchmaker Flower."

Random Notes on Reading Paintings

—Jiang Taihua

Since the Qing Dynasty, the painters of Yangzhou have first counted Wang Su Xiaomou, and the two families who competed with him are Shi Lianxi and Ye Hang. The two families both took the law from Xinluo. Xiaomou's brushwork is better than unrestrained, and the coloring is better than elegant. Ye Hang Nai avoids his strengths and specializes in being profound to seek vividness. Gu Zhangjilan is an indoor disciple of Ye Hang, and also takes the best of Xiaomou. Therefore, he was already famous at the age of thirty. In his middle age, he reached a more exquisite state. Zhang still thought it was not enough, and devoted himself to hard work. Now, even though he is over seventy years old, he still paints every day as a routine, so every time he puts down his pen, the later sages all respectfully praise him and feel that he cannot reach it. I have been friends with the scholar Tianzan, the son of a philosopher, for a long time. I have obtained three paintings by Zhang. One is a poem about writing cranes and Qin books on the same boat. The spring water is rising and the wave marks are alive. The plum blossoms are blooming on both sides. A small boat is leisurely between them. A guest is sitting in the middle, twisting his beard and looking up to the sky, smiling, with the fun of being outside the world, and the cranes and the children on the boat are all looking back with affection, unlike those who do not belong to each other. One is a mountain temple bell sound, with pine waves and cloud shadows. A monk is carrying a bamboo hat and returning halfway up the mountain. Above the halfway point, it is sealed by clouds. Only the corner of the Vatican palace is revealed on the pine peak outside the ridge. The sound of the bell cannot be painted, but there is a returning monk to show the time when the bell is ringing, and the Vatican palace to show the place where the bell is ringing, and the sound of the bell is faintly audible in the ear unintentionally. One writes about peach blossoms and pheasants. A white peach blossom is graceful and precious like a Han palace person. Two pheasants are facing each other on the branches, wanting to sing. The spring air is full of paper, and the color is bright and extremely fresh, which is very different from the old man's pen. Although the paintings by Zhang that I have collected are only a few, they do not fully capture Zhang's abilities. However, the characters, landscapes, flowers, and birds are all prepared, and the creation of the environment, sketching, and setting of colors are all excellent. How can those who imitate them hope to reach his back? In the summer of Xinwei, Zhang will hold a hundred recent works at the same time as Huang Jun Hanhou's bamboo carving exhibition in Shanghai, which can add a lot of color to the art world. In the past, Gu Changkang was called the three absolutes for his talent, painting, and madness. Zhang has no madness like Changkang, but his painting name has been promoted from one county to the whole country. Not only can he follow the ancestral martial arts, but also surpass his predecessors.

Rambling Talks on Traveling in Korea (9)

—Ji Ping

Since the overseas Chinese in Korea are in a superior position, the number of people from China who go to Korea to make a living is increasing day by day. The Japanese, seeing this situation, have come up with various methods to restrict the entry of overseas Chinese, repel those who have already entered, or instruct a group of Japanese and Korean vagrants to bully overseas Chinese. It is said that this group of vagrants often publicly insults them on the prosperous streets and provokes them for no reason. People are not made of wood or stone, who would be willing to suffer losses in front of their eyes? Who would be willing to lose the face of the country? If they show a little resistance, they will be scolded and beaten. If you call the police, he will stand by and ignore you. You have no choice but to hold back your tears and swallow your anger and escape from their circle. Where can you go to complain? It is only because the motherland is not prosperous that no one will protect you. Therefore, overseas Chinese cannot rely on their families or the country, but only "rely on God for food."

The number of unemployed people in Korea has been increasing in recent years. The Governor-General's Office nominally provides relief to the poor Korean people who are unemployed, but it is actually actively repelling our innocent overseas Chinese. Since April 1 of this year, it has proposed a total budget of 65 million Japanese yen to complete the plan in three years, such as water management, road repairs, and port construction in various provinces, counties, and prefectures, so that unemployed Koreans can have work to do and avoid becoming bandits and disturbing the local area. It also established a mutual aid organization for Korean workers and formulated a secret order to restrict the use of Chinese workers. It was found that this kind of secret order is not only implemented in various government-run projects, but also in individual contracting businesses. In the treaty ports, only one-fifth or less of the workers used in factories are allowed to be Chinese workers, and the local police authorities in various provinces, prefectures, counties, and townships issue police orders based on domestic law and the proposals of autonomous organizations to force Chinese workers to obtain labor permits before they can work hard under their strict restrictions. The conditions for obtaining a permit are very harsh, such as (1) the application for a permit must be written in Japanese, (2) a health certificate from a Japanese doctor must be obtained first, and (3) only one year of work is allowed. After the expiration, all the above conditions must be fulfilled again to apply for a permit. Therefore, although the general foremen and landlords want to hire cheap and hardworking Chinese workers, they are restricted by the harsh conditions of the officialdom and have the suffering of being unable to help. Since the promulgation of this secret order, Chinese workers have been unemployed and wandering in foreign countries, which is very pitiful. Our country's government has never heard of any relief measures, and it does not care about the lives of overseas Chinese or the face of the country, which is really a very painful fact.

Since the Japanese are so harsh on our overseas Chinese, we should naturally return this kind of equivalent condition to them. It is not too much in reason and emotion. According to the latest survey, the ratio of overseas Chinese in Japan and Korea to Japanese and Korean overseas Chinese in China is as follows:

Overseas Chinese in Japan 25,963 people Japanese overseas Chinese in China 158,867 people Overseas Chinese in Korea 91,466 people Korean overseas Chinese in China 599,890 people (Among them, two-thirds are Korean overseas Chinese in Yanji, Helong, Wangqing, Hunchun, Fusong, Antu, and other counties, that is, the so-called Jian Island area, which are Korean overseas Chinese who are the vanguard of the Japanese. The remaining one-third are Korean overseas Chinese scattered in Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and other provinces.)

Total number of Japanese and Korean overseas Chinese 117,429 people Total number of Japanese and Korean overseas Chinese in China 758,757 people Comparative difference 641,297 people

From the above figures, it can be seen that the number of Japanese and Korean expatriates living in China is 641,297 more than the number of Chinese expatriates living in Japan and Korea, almost six times more. In the future, unless both parties respect the equal and mutually beneficial commercial treaty, we will never allow them to abuse us like cattle and horses, while we treat them like honored guests. We will never tolerate this unequal treatment again. Before the new Sino-Japanese commercial treaty is signed, it is hoped that our diplomatic authorities will carefully consider this point and the issue of Korean naturalization in order to achieve a permanent effect.

Rotary Club Novel

??? (26)

—Xu Zhuodai

Ziliang thought to himself: Who wants to drink tea? If I had known it was for myself, I wouldn't have bothered to pour it.

"I don't want to drink!"

"You must drink!"

Ziliang was afraid of arguing with her, so he drank the tea in one gulp.

"Turn on the light!"

The order from the Internal Affairs Department came down again. Ziliang saw that it was indeed getting dark, so he went to the door and turned on the light.

"Go tell the nanny: I can't eat dinner, I want porridge."

Ziliang seemed to be a servant of the lady, being sent around by her. He went downstairs and told the nanny, then went back upstairs to the room to see that the lady didn't look sick, so he felt relieved and quietly went to the pavilion to turn on the light and do his official business. Today, he has revised a total of eight or nine articles. Even if he works late into the night, it will be difficult to finish the more than one hundred and sixty books. At most, he can get rid of half of them, so he has to do as much as he can. Ziliang was revising the first article when he suddenly heard a strange cry in the room:

"Not good!"

This was the lady's cry of surprise. Ziliang threw down his pen and rushed to the room and saw the lady sitting in the middle of the bed, pointing to the coat rack:

"There's a ghost! There's a ghost!"

Her eyes showed horror, as if the ghost was standing in the room.

"Don't be scared! Don't be scared! There's nothing, I'm here."

Although Ziliang was comforting her, she still cried out in surprise:

"Look! There's a white ghost over there!"

"No! Where?"

"Right here!"

Commercial News

Finance

Gold Price Initially Rises, Then Declines

Optimism Regarding German Debt

Market Sentiment Suddenly Turns Negative

Fluctuations Extremely Strong: Yesterday, the 18th, the benchmark gold price rose and then fell, with considerable volatility. Between the morning and noon, there were over eight taels of discrepancies, creating a confusing situation. Ultimately, it fell slightly by one and a half taels. The silver market fell back, and while US stocks showed a slight increase, they did not cause much influence. Therefore, the gold price, which had initially risen, pushed past the 750-tael mark but was then met with strong selling pressure. Speculators and Dalian banks frequently sold off. As the foreign exchange rate strengthened and then weakened, with covert stability, the gold price turned downward, sharply reducing by seven or eight taels, retreating within 50 taels, with only three or four taels of fluctuation. Finally, it closed at 47 taels and zero. The afternoon was closed due to Saturday. Recalling the market conditions this week, it has become a winding situation, coinciding with the German loan news being divergent, and since the September term entered the market, the trend has been upward. In the last three days, the difference between the high and low prices has been 22 taels and 4 qian. Compared to the initial opening price on the morning of the 16th, it has increased by 7 taels and 5 qian. The market situation yesterday is recorded below:

The Opening Price Pushes Through the 50-Tael Mark: The September opening price started by adding three taels, reaching 751 taels and a half. Large bars fell back by a quarter. Public and private telegrams both showed a decrease of 3/8 in the silver price. However, the market was stable. Subsequently, due to selling activity, it immediately dropped to 48 taels. Then, a sharp rise began as HSBC bought English gold at 1875, Mitsubishi sold 125, and Fuchang and others purchased from Zhengjin and Shanghai at prices ranging from .0625 to .125. With the efforts of Qianchangxiang and Dadecheng, it jumped by six or seven taels, reaching 54 taels and 9 qian. After that, Fuyu and Yuanmaoyong began selling, suppressing the price to 51 taels and a half. When the English gold announcement was released, it had shrunk by 125, US dollars by 375, and Japanese gold added 1.75 fen, causing the price to rise to 52 taels and 8 qian. However, Mitsui and others sold English gold at 125, and Zhifeng, Yongqianchangxiang, Yuanmaoyong, and other major players sold off, causing the price to plummet by more than five taels, breaking the 50-tael mark. Wanxing and others also sold, reaching 10.0 at 47 taels. Around 10:30, the price on the board was 50 taels. Because retail investors were buying and Sumitomo bought spot Dalian at 1 tael, 6 qian, and 1 fen, it dropped to 47 taels, 7 or 8 qian around 10:50. Suddenly, the banks bought English gold at 125 to 1875, causing it to jump up by 4 taels again, and hedging came in, reaching 52 taels at 11:10. Unexpectedly, the banks were willing to sell English gold again, totaling 125 to 1875. Around 11:30, it was 48 taels, 6 or 7 qian, immediately rising to 50 taels, 6 or 7 qian, with the state being unstable.

Sharp Decline Approaching Closing: Later, the Dalian banks, Yuanmao, Tianxiang, Yuanchun, and others all sold off. It was also rumored that German debt matters might be optimistic, and the market sentiment suddenly turned negative. In just seven or eight minutes, it dropped by four taels, ending at 46 taels and 5 qian. In an instant, it pulled up to 2 taels, reaching 8 taels and 3 qian. When the noon closing came, it was 47 taels, then suppressed again to 6 taels and a half, then raised again to outside of 7 taels. Compared to the previous day (according to the listed price), it fell by 1 tael and a half. Silk and Tea

Doubles Silk Exports are Subject to Special Tax

Same Treatment as Jiangsu and Zhejiang Factories... Taxed 30 Yuan Per Package Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Industry Public Bonds are Issued with Terms Doubles Silk Factories Have Been Approved to Enjoy the Right to Dispose of Public Bonds, Receiving the Same Treatment as Jiangsu and Zhejiang Singles Silk Factories. The Local Jianghai Customs Has Been Ordered to Collect Special Taxes on All Double Silk Exports at 30 Yuan Per Package from the Date of Promulgation of the Silk Industry Public Bond Regulations to be Used to Allocate Public Bond Funds. The Goods Inspection Bureau Will Determine the Export Quantity of Doubles Silk that was Previously Not Subject to Special Tax and Instruct Each Factory to Supplement it. Therefore, Doubles Silk Exports are Subject to Special Taxes.

Oil Market

White Tung Oil Appears to Have Stabilized

Since the sudden rise in Hankou white tung oil the previous week, foreign firms have sold at a maximum of 24 taels and 7 mace per unit. Upon investigation, the reason is that the supply is scarce and domestic sales are appropriate. As such, foreign firms have also slightly increased their outlets at this time, and transactions are slightly brisk. Due to cost considerations, customers have all reacted quickly. In three to four days, the price has risen by as much as two taels. However, foreign firms do not have large stocks, and seeing the market price rise, they have hesitated. Therefore, it soon fell back. According to recent reports from Hankou, it has relaxed to 23 taels and 4 mace. In recent years, local firms have mainly focused on Zhejiang tung oil, and Hankou oil is rare. However, the market still looks to Hankou as its leader. Therefore, Hangzhou also echoed the increase in Hankou tung oil, increasing from 31 yuan per dan to 35 yuan repeatedly, all delivered to Shanghai. However, buyers still find the price too expensive, so transactions are very few. Recently, due to the decline in the Hankou market, Zhejiang tung oil has also followed suit, relaxing to 33 yuan and 45 cents. The market seems to have stabilized at this point, and buyers also do not want the price to be too low. It is heard that upland customers seem to have a slight intention to buy at this price. If it is cheaper, they would rather store it than sell it. Based on this, the current market can be temporarily stabilized and there should be no further changes. However, the time is approaching the hot season, which is the peak sales season. If sales in various places start, then it will be another matter. Local firms' inventories are neither too thick nor too thin, but sales during the peak season will inevitably be slightly more than usual.

Shanghai Market

Market News

The Daxin Silk and Satin Store at the corner of Third Ma Road and Stone Road proclaims that since the beginning of summer, its goods have been selling well and business has been exceptionally prosperous. To establish itself as a unique presence in the silk and satin industry, the store has specially woven a type of printed Parisian gauze never before seen in Shanghai. In recent days, the store has received the goods, featuring no fewer than dozens of novel patterns. This fabric is light, brightly colored, inexpensive, and of high quality, unmatched by any other fashionable fabric in Shanghai. It truly deserves to be called a modern masterpiece. Socialites have been rushing to purchase this fabric in recent days, considering it an essential garment for summer social events.

The Dachang Silk and Satin Store at the intersection of Third Ma Road and Stone Road announces that the store has been in business for over ten years, with a well-deserved reputation for authentic goods at fair prices. This year, due to the need to rebuild the store's premises, all goods are being sold at discounted prices. With the demolition date drawing near, and a large quantity of inventory remaining unsold, the store is further reducing prices by 70% to expedite clearance. This major price reduction, disregarding all costs, is a rare opportunity to purchase affordable silk and satin. It is hoped that all sectors will not miss out on this opportunity.

The Jinlong Vegetable Company at the corner of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road proclaims that the jade dew peaches produced by the Zhejiang Changxing Senshen Afforestation Farm, which are managed and sold by the company, have been met with extremely enthusiastic purchases and thriving sales since being transported to Shanghai from their place of origin and advertised in the newspapers. This has created an unprecedented sales record for fruit. This is because the peaches are large, juicy, and extremely sweet, surpassing all other types of flat peaches on the market.

Theater News

The Mingxing Film Company announces that since the release of its first sound film, "Songstress Red Peony," the results have been excellent and universally praised. Recently, director Zhang Shichuan has continued directing a second sound film, "Such Is Paradise," which has been in production for some time. Most of the filming is already complete, and the company is currently focusing on sound recording. The film is expected to be completed within the month. The film is even more spectacular than "Red Peony." When it is released on the silver screen, it will surely create a sensation.

The Hua Ju Film Company announces that its production, "Nine Deaths and One Life," directed by villainous star Sheng Xiaotian, has finally been completed after several months of exhaustive effort. The plot of the film is bizarre and shocking, full of unresolved mysteries. It is deeply embedded with detective elements and contains various aspects of tragedy, comedy, horror, and wonder. The film has now been completed and will be released soon. Manager Zhang Huimin believes that film art can be used to promote culture and assist education. In addition to careful research, he has specially hired theater and film artist Wan Laitian to create a film with a noble plot and profound meaning, tasked with promoting women's education and promoting national spirit. The lead role is played by Ding Yuming, a tragic star admired by millions, and is assisted by martial arts star Zhang Huimin and over a hundred female students from various schools, further enhancing the film's quality and appeal. The company is working diligently to complete the production, which is expected to be finished soon.

Medical Information

Yu Xuan Medicine Company proclaims that Mr. Zhang, residing on Jin Shenfu Road, suffered from a cough for more than a month. Fortunately, after taking one box of "Long-Term Cough Tablets" issued by this pharmacy at the West Scissors Bridge Road branch of the Local Office, the coughing subsided. After taking two more boxes, the cough completely disappeared. These tablets are also sold at the Lixing Steamship Bureau near the Pentang Bridge, the Shuncheng Credit Bureau on Li Xian Gua Street in the South City, Bao Da Hao at the intersection of Xinzha Road and Changsha Road, the Yixing Hao on Dada Tou Street, the Tongfaxiang Hao near the South City Train Station, and the distribution department of the Xinwen Bao newspaper. Patients can purchase the tablets nearby for six jiao of silver dollars per box.

Home
